kailāsaśikharāsīnaṃ bhairavaṃ vigatāmayam 
caṇḍanandimahākāla gaṇeśavṛṣabhṛṅgibhiḥ  SvaT 
kumārendrayamāditya brahmaviṣṇupuraḥsaraiḥ 
stūyamānaṃ maheśānaṃ gaṇamātṛniṣevitam  SvaT 
sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartāraṃ vilayasthitakārakam 
anugrahakaraṃ devaṃ praṇatārtivināśanam  SvaT 
muditaṃ bhairavaṃ dṛṣṭvā devī vacanamabravīt 
śrīdevyuvāca
yattvayā kathitaṃ mahyaṃ svacchandaṃ parameśvara  SvaT 
śatakoṭipravistīrṇaṃ bhedānantyavisarpitam 
catuṣpīṭhaṃ mahātantra catuṣṭayaphalodayam  SvaT 
na śaknuvanti manujā alpavīryaparākramāḥ 
alpāyuṣo 'lpavittāśca alpasattvāśca śaṃkara  SvaT 
tadarthaṃ saṃgrahaṃ tasya svalpaśāstrārthavistaram 
bhuktimuktipradātāraṃ kathayasva prasādataḥ  SvaT 
kīdṛśaṃ vai guruṃ vidyāt sādhakaṃ ca maheśvara 
bhayābhayapradātāraṃ śiṣyaṃ bhūmiṃ ca kīdṛśīm  SvaT 
mantrāṃścaiva samāsena kālaṃ caiva samāsataḥ 
yajanaṃ havanaṃ caiva adhivāsaṃ rajāṃsi ca  SvaT 
pañcagavyaṃ caruṃ caiva dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca maṇḍalam 
dīkṣā cādhvābhiṣekau ca samayānsādhanāni ca  SvaT 
kalimāsādya sidhyanti tathā brūhi maheśvara 
śrībhairava uvāca
sādhu sādhu mahābhāge yattvayā paricoditam  SvaT 
anugrahāya martyānāṃ sāmprataṃ kathayāmi te 
ādau tāvatparīkṣeta ācāryaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam  SvaT 
āryadeśasamutpannaṃ sarvāvayavabhūṣitam 
śivaśāstravidhānajñaṃ jñānajñeyaviśāradam  SvaT 
devakarmarataṃ śāntaṃ satyavādidṛḍhavratam 
sattvavadvīryasampannaṃ dayādākṣiṇyasaṃyutam  SvaT 
tyāginaṃ dambhanirmuktaṃ śivaśāstreṣu bhāvitam 
īdṛśaṃ tu guruṃ prāpya siddhimuktī na dūrataḥ  SvaT 
krodhanaścapalaḥ kṣudro dayādākṣiṇyavarjitaḥ 
kekaro danturaḥ kāṇaḥ pāpiṣṭhaḥ śāstravarjitaḥ  SvaT 
atidīrghastathā hrasvaḥ kṛśaḥ sthūlaḥ kṣayānvitaḥ 
tārkiko dambhasaṃyuktaḥ satyaśaucavivarjitaḥ  SvaT 
anyaśāstrarato yastu nāsau muktiphalapradaḥ 
śiṣyo dayānvito dhīro dambhamāyāvivarjitaḥ  SvaT 
devāgnigurubhaktaśca śāstrabhakto dṛḍhavrataḥ 
guruśuśrūṣaṇaparaḥ suśāntendriyasaṃyutaḥ  SvaT 
īdṛśo vai bhavecchiṣyaḥ so 'trānugrahabhājanam 
māyānvitaḥ śaṭhaḥ krūro niḥsatyaḥ kalahapriyaḥ  SvaT 
kāmī ca lobhasampannaḥ śivabhaktivivarjitaḥ 
dūṣako guruśāstrāṇāṃ dīkṣito 'pi na muktibhāk  SvaT 
santāpaṃ krodhane vindyāc capale capalāḥ śriyaḥ 
mantrasiddhiṃ haret kṣudra ācāryastu varānane  SvaT 
dayāhīnena daurbhāgyam adakṣe dasyupīḍanam 
kekareṇa bhavedvyādhir danturaḥ kalikārakaḥ  SvaT 
kāṇo vidveṣajananaḥ khalvāṭaścārthanāśanaḥ 
śāstrahīne na siddhiḥ syād dīkṣādau vīravandite  SvaT 
dīrghe rājabhayaṃ jñeyaṃ hrasvaḥ putravināśanaḥ 
kṛśaḥ kṣayakaro jñeyaḥ sthūla utpātakārakaḥ  SvaT 
kṣayānvitena mṛtyuḥ syāt tārkike vadhabandhanam 
dāmbhikaḥ pāpajanako veditavyo varānane  SvaT 
mantāstasya na siddhyanti yaḥ satyādivivarjitaḥ 
sarve te na śubhā devi iha loke paratra ca  SvaT 
sitaraktapītakṛṣṇāṃ bhūmiṃ plavaviśodhitām 
viśalyāṃ lakṣaṇairyuktāṃ sarvakāmārthasādhikām  SvaT 
sugandhigandhasaṃyuktāṃ puṣpaprakaralālitām 
sudhūpāmodabahalāṃ vitānopariśobhitam  SvaT 
ācāryastu śucirbhūtvā candanāgurucarcitaḥ 
sudhūpitaḥ prasannātmā khaṭikākarasaṃyutaḥ  SvaT 
prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ 
mātṛkāṃ prastarettatra ādikṣāntāmanukramāt  SvaT 
ādiḥ ṣoḍaśabhedena sākṣādvai bhairavaḥ smṛtaḥ 
kavargaścaṭavargau ca tapayāḥ śastathaiva ca  SvaT 
saṃhāreṇa samopetau yonirvai bhairavī smṛtā 
mātṛkābhairavaṃ devam avargeṇa prapūjayet  SvaT 
bhairavī kādinā pūjyā mātṛvargaiḥ prapūjayet 
avarge tu mahālakṣmīḥ kavarge kamalodbhavā  SvaT 
cavarge tu maheśānī ṭavarge tu kumārikā 
nārāyaṇī tavarge tu vārāhī tu pavargikā  SvaT 
aindrī caiva yavargasthā cāmuṇḍā tu śavargikā 
etāḥ sapta mahāmātṛḥ saptalokavyavasthitāḥ  SvaT 
sarvān kāmānavāpnoti devyevaṃ bhairavo 'bravīt 
ante 'sya uddharenmantrān yathākramaniyogataḥ  SvaT 
trayodaśaṃ binduyutam anantāsanamuttamam 
anena yojayetsarvaṃ somasūryāgnimadhyagam  SvaT 
brahmaviṣṇumaheśānaṃ śavāntaṃ parikalpayet 
mūrtiṃ haṃsākṣareṇaiva bindubhinnena kalpayet  SvaT 
ardhacandrakṛtāṭopāṃ svasvanāṃ tuhinaprabhām 
tadūrdhve sakalaṃ devaṃ svacchandaṃ parikalpayet  SvaT 
oṃkāramuccaretpūrvam aghorebhyo anantaram 
tha ghorebhyo samālikhya tato 'nyattu samālikhet  SvaT 
ghoraghoratarebhyaśca sarvataḥ śarva uccaret 
sarvebhyaḥ padamanyacca namaste rudra eva ca  SvaT 
rūpebhyaśca samālikhya namaskārāvasānakam 
mantrarājaḥ samākhyātaḥ aghoraḥ surapūjitaḥ  SvaT 
sakṛduccārito devi nāśayet sarvakilbiṣam 
janmakoṭīsahasraistu bhramadbhiḥ samupārjitam  SvaT 
smaraṇānnāśayeddevi tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā 
yakārādivakārāntāḥ saṃhāreṇa samāyutāḥ  SvaT 
bindumastakasambhinnā bhairavasya mukhāni ca 
brahmabhaṅgyā niyojyāni mūrdhādicaraṇāvadhi  SvaT 
punaścordhvaṃ mukhaṃ kalpyaṃ prāgdakṣiṇamathottaram 
aparaṃ kalpayitvā tu kalābhedena vinyaset  SvaT 
pūrvaṃ ca dakṣiṇaṃ caiva uttaraṃ paścimaṃ tathā 
ūrdhvamūrdhnā tu saṃyuktaṃ kṣakāraṃ tvīśarūpiṇam  SvaT 
evaṃ vaktraṃ caturdhā tu vaktreṣveva niyojayet 
pañcamaṃ yadbhavedvaktraṃ kṣakāreṇaiva nirdiśet  SvaT 
hṛdi grīvāṃsapṛṣṭhe tu nābhau ca jaṭhare tathā 
pṛṣṭhe corasi vinyased aghoreṇa yathākramam  SvaT 
guhye tathā gude caiva tathorvorjānunorapi 
jaṅghayośca sphijoḥ kaṭyāṃ pārśvayorubhayorapi  SvaT 
vinyaseccaiva vāmena śarīre tu yathākramam 
pādau hastau tathā nāsāṃ śiraścaiva bhujāvatha  SvaT 
sadyena kalpayeddevi sarvametadyathākramam 
tāsāṃ nāmāni vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  SvaT 
tārā sutārā taraṇī tārayantī sutāraṇī 
īśānasya kalā pañca nirañjanapadānugā  SvaT 
nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhā ca vidyā śāntistathaiva ca 
puruṣasya kalā hyetāś catasraḥ parikīrtitāḥ  SvaT 
tamā mohā kṣudhā nidrā mṛtyurmāyā bhayā jarā 
aghorasya kalā hyetā aṣṭau vai varavarṇini  SvaT 
rajā rakṣā ratiḥ pālyā kāmyā tṛṣṇā matiḥ kriyā 
ṛddhirmāyā ca rātriśca bhrāmiṇī mohanī tathā  SvaT 
manonmanī kalā hyetā vāmadeve trayodaśa 
siddhirṛddhirdyutirlakṣmīr medhā kāntiḥ sudhā sthitiḥ  SvaT 
sadyojātakalāstvevam aṣṭau samparikīrtitāḥ 
punaśca sādhako devi sarvāṅgeṣu yathākramam  SvaT 
navatattvaṃ tritattvaṃ ca dhruveṇa parikalpayet 
vidyāṅgāni punarnyasya teṣāṃ mantrān śṛṇu priye  SvaT 
aghorebhyo samālikhya tha ghorebhyo dvitīyakam 
ghoraghoratarebhyaśca tṛtīyaṃ parikalpayet  SvaT 
sarvataḥ śarva sarvebhyo caturthaṃ parikalpayet 
namaste rudrarūpebhyaḥ pañcamaṃ ca vidhānataḥ  SvaT 
oṃkāramuccaretpūrvaṃ juṃ saśca tadanantaram 
netratrayaṃ prakalpeta vidyādehasya bhāmini  SvaT 
vidyāṅgāni vijānīyāt nāmāni ca nibodha me 
sarvātmā tu brahmaśiro jvālinī piṅgalaṃ tathā  SvaT 
durbhedyaṃ pāśupatyaṃ ca jyotīrūpaṃ tathaiva ca 
kriyā jñānaṃ tathaivecchā tāsāṃ mantrānnibodha me  SvaT 
caturthasvarasaṃyuktaṃ hāntaṃ binduvibhūṣitam 
kriyāśaktiḥ samākhyātā sarvasṛṣṭiprakāśikā  SvaT 
śakārasya tṛtīyaṃ tu ṣaṣṭhayuktaṃ sabindukam 
jñānaśaktiḥ smṛtā hyeṣā prabodhajananī śubhā  SvaT 
kṣādiṃ dvisvarasambhinnaṃ tripañcena tu mūrchitam 
icchāśaktiḥ samākhyātā bhairavasyāmitātmikā  SvaT 
haṃsākhyo bindusaṃyuktaḥ ṣaṣṭhasvaravibheditaḥ 
bālendunādaśaktyantaḥ svacchando niṣkalaḥ smṛtaḥ  SvaT 
asyoccaraṇamātreṇa ye yuktāḥ sarvapātakaiḥ 
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśāḥ padaṃ gacchantyanāmayam  SvaT 
sāntaṃ dīrghasvaraiḥ ṣaḍbhir bhinnajātivibheditam 
hṛcchiraśca śikhā varma locanāstraṃ prakalpayet  SvaT 
oṃkāro dīpanasteṣām ante jātiṃ prakalpayet 
namaḥ svāhā tathā vauṣaṭ huṃ vaṣaṭ phaṭ krameṇa tu  SvaT 
eṣa bhairavarājastu sarvakāmārthasādhakaḥ 
hara īma akāraśca ṅādirosvarasaṃyutaḥ  SvaT 
yānta ekārasaṃyuktaḥ ṣādirlāntavibheditaḥ 
lādistrisvarasambhinno haṃso bindusamāyuktaḥ  SvaT 
ṣaṣṭhasvarasamopetaḥ phaṭkārāntavikalpitaḥ 
aghoreśvarīti vikhyātā svacchandotsaṅgagāminī  SvaT 
bhairavāṅgasamopetā vaktrapañcakasaṃyutā 
hānto yādiryakārānto rādiḥ ṣaṣṭhakalānvitaḥ  SvaT 
bindunādasamāyogāt kapāleśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
sānto binduradho hyagniḥ ṣaṣṭhayuktastu kīrtitaḥ  SvaT 
śikhivāhanasaṃjñastu jñātavyo 'sau varānane 
saṃhāraḥ ṣaṣṭhasaṃyuktaḥ ṣaḍantena samanvitaḥ  SvaT 
krodharājaḥ samākhyātaḥ         
        tathānyaṃ kathayāmi te 
ñādiḥ ṣaṣṭhasvaropetas tripadena samāyutaḥ  SvaT 
bindumastakasambhinno vikarālo varānane 
sāntaḥ śādyena saṃyuktaḥ ṣaṣṭhasvarayuto 'pyadhaḥ  SvaT 
caturdaśasvarākrānto bindunādāntabhūṣitaḥ 
manmathaḥ kathito hyeṣa surasiddhanamaskṛtaḥ  SvaT 
yenedaṃ tu nijaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam 
hararādisamāyuktaḥ ūkārādhaḥ sabindukaḥ  SvaT 
meghanādeśvaro hyeṣa bhairavaḥ samprakīrtitaḥ 
kṣasāntarbindusaṃyuktaḥ pañcamena vibheditaḥ  SvaT 
someśvaraḥ samākhyāto janmamṛtyuvināśanaḥ 
kṣādiryāntasamopeto hāntenādhoniyojitaḥ  SvaT 
bhānto vādirlakārānto rādyo 'dho rudrayojitaḥ 
bindvardhendusamāyukto nādaśaktisamanvitaḥ  SvaT 
vidyārājaḥ samākhyāto mahāpātakanāśanaḥ 
bhairavāṣṭakametaddhi parivāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ  SvaT 
lokapālāṃstathoddhṛtya svanāmapraṇavādikān 
namaskārāvamānāṃśca sāstrānsamparikalpayet  SvaT 
iti svacchandatantre mantroddhāraprakāśanaṃ nāma prathamaḥ paṭalaḥ
dvitīyaḥ paṭalaḥ
athārcanaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ 
śaucaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ snānaṃ kartavyaṃ tu mṛdambhasā  SvaT 
śucisthānānmṛdaṃ pūrvaṃ gṛhītvāstreṇa śodhitām 
prakṣālya jalatīraṃ tu sthāpayettāṃ varānane  SvaT 
bhāgadvayaṃ tato 'streṇa kartavyaṃ tu kṛśodari 
bhāgārdhena kaṭiṃ corū jaṅghe pādau tathaiva ca  SvaT 
kṣālayeta yathānyāyaṃ trirantaritayogataḥ 
avaśiṣṭaṃ tu bhāgārdhaṃ gṛhītvāstrābhimantritam  SvaT 
saptavārānvarārohe arkadīptaṃ tu kārayet 
śiraḥprabhṛti pādāntam āguṣṭhya snānamācaret  SvaT 
uttīryodakamadhyāttu upaspṛśya yathākramam 
saṃdhyāyā vandanaṃ kuryāc chāstradṛṣṭena karmaṇā  SvaT 
malasnānaṃ bhavedevaṃ vidhisnānaṃ pracakṣmahe 
bhāgārdhaṃ yatsthitaṃ pūrvaṃ tato bhāgatrayaṃ kuru  SvaT 
vāmahastasya pūrve ca dakṣiṇe cottare kramāt 
pūrvabhāgaṃ tato 'streṇa saptavārāṃstu mantrayet  SvaT 
dakṣiṇasthaṃ tathā vaktrair abhimantrya varānane 
uttaraṃ cābhimantryaivaṃ devenāṅgayutena ca  SvaT 
pūrvabhāgaṃ gṛhītvā tu daśadikṣu vinikṣipet 
uttareṇa tu bhāgena jalaṃ caivābhimantrayet  SvaT 
bāhumātrapramāṇena bhairaveśamanusmaran 
ātmānaṃ guṇṭhayitvā tu dakṣabhāgena suvrate  SvaT 
snāyādrājopacāreṇa sugandhāmalakādibhiḥ 
prāṇāyāmābhiṣekau tu kartavyau bhairaveṇa ca  SvaT 
uttīryodakamadhyāttu tadvāsaḥ parivartayet 
upaspṛśya kṛtanyāso mūlamantramanusmaran  SvaT 
tīrthaṃ saṃgṛhya deveśi ātmano 'gre nidhāpayet 
tatrastho vandayetsaṃdhyāṃ mārjanādiranukramāt  SvaT 
aghamarṣaḥ prakartavya upasthānaṃ divākare 
japaṃ kṛtvā nivedyaivaṃ praṇamya ca varānane  SvaT 
mantrāṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā devānāmṛṣibhiḥ saha 
sarveṣāṃ bhūtasaṃghānāṃ tatastīrthaṃ tu saṃharet  SvaT 
mūlamantramanusmṛtya bhasmasnānamataḥ param 
malasnānaṃ prakartavyaṃ bhāvitenāntarātmanā  SvaT 
parivṛttya tato vāsaḥ saṃdhyāṃ prāgiva vandayet 
vidhisnānaṃ tataḥ kuryād bhairaveśamanusmaran  SvaT 
śiro vaktraṃ ca hṛdguhyaṃ pādāntaṃ ca vibhāgaśaḥ 
bhairaveṇāṅgayuktena samuddhūlyaṃ yathākramam  SvaT 
abhiṣekaṃ prakurvīta paraṃ tattvamanusmaran 
saṃdhyāyā vandanaṃ kuryād yathāpūrvaṃ varānane  SvaT 
tato yāgagṛhaṃ gatvā hastau pādau ca kṣālayet 
śikhāṃ baddhvā śikhāṃ smṛtvā upaspṛśya vidhānataḥ  SvaT 
sakalīkṛtadehastu puṣpamādāya suvrate 
diṅmātṛbhyo namaskṛtya dvāraṃ saṃprokṣya yatnataḥ  SvaT 
śivāmbhasāstramantreṇa vighnaproccāṭanaṃ bhavet 
dvāraśākhordhvato devaṃ gaṇeśaṃ ca śriyaṃ tathā  SvaT 
saṃpūjya gandhapuṣpādyair dhūpādibhiranukramāt 
arghyapādyopahāraiśca tato dvārasya cottare  SvaT 
nandigaṅge samabhyarcya mahākālaṃ ca dakṣiṇe 
kālindīṃ caiva saṃpūjya yathānukramayogataḥ  SvaT 
bhairavāstraṃ samuccārya puṣpaṃ saṃgṛhya bhāvitaḥ 
saptābhimantritaṃ kṛtvā jvaladagniśikhākulam  SvaT 
nārācāstraprayogeṇa praviśedgṛhamadhyataḥ 
nivāritaṃ tena sarvaṃ vighnajālamanantakam  SvaT 
tato rakṣārthamantraṃ ca daśadikṣu vinikṣipet 
madhye sampūjya brahmāṇaṃ gandhaiḥ puṣpairanukramāt  SvaT 
dakṣiṇāyāṃ tato mūrtau praṇavāsanasaṃsthitaḥ 
upaviśyāsanaṃ baddhvā svabhyastaṃ vai puraḥsthitam  SvaT 
gandhadigdhau karau kṛtvā astreṇa pariśodhayet 
kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaitau plāvayedamṛtena tu  SvaT 
parāṃ śaktiṃ tu saṃkṣobhya tato 'nantaṃ prakalpayet 
mūrtiṃ nyasyānuvaktrāṇi svacchandaṃ parikalpayet  SvaT 
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ vinyasedaṅgapañcakam 
bhairavānapi saṃkalpya paraṃ tattvamanusmaret  SvaT 
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kāryaṃ dehasaṃśuddhikāraṇam 
aśuddhaḥ svamarudrecyaḥ śuddhenāpūrayettanum  SvaT 
kumbhakaṃ recakaṃ kṛtvā vyomnyātmānaṃ nidhāpayet 
khadyotakanibhaṃ sūkṣmaṃ karaṇaistu vivarjitam  SvaT 
kāryeṇaiva vihīnaṃ ca māyāpradhvastagocaram 
śivīkāryastathātmaiva yathā bhavati tacchṛṇu  SvaT 
paraṃ bhāvaṃ tu saṃgṛhya tataḥ śoṣyā tanuḥ priye 
saṃhāreṇa yabhinnena rudrabījayutena ca  SvaT 
tenaiva dahanaṃ kāryam ūrdhvādho 'gniyutena ca 
adho viṣṇusamāyukto vāyuvarṇaḥ sabindukaḥ  SvaT 
utpūyanakaro hyeṣa plāvane vāruṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
bindumastakasaṃbhinnaḥ śaktinyāsastato bhavet  SvaT 
ānayettaṃ yathānītaṃ plāvayedamṛtena tu 
malapradhvastacaitanyaṃ kalāvidyāsamāśritam  SvaT 
rāgeṇa rañjitātmāna kālena kalitaṃ tathā 
niyatyā yamitaṃ bhūyaḥ puṃbhāvenopabṛṃhitam  SvaT 
pradhānāśayasaṃpannaṃ guṇatrayasamanvitam 
buddhitattvasamāsīnam ahaṅkārasamāvṛtam  SvaT 
manasā buddhikarmākṣais tanmātraiḥ sthūlabhūtakaiḥ 
praṇavena tu sarvaṃ tac charīrotpattikāraṇam  SvaT 
nyasetkrameṇa deveśi triṃśadekaṃ ca saṃkhyayā 
ṣaṭtattvī tvātmasaṃbaddhā jñātavyātra varānane  SvaT 
pradhānāvaniparyantaṃ śarīraṃ ca vinirmitam 
caturviṃśatitattvāni caitanyarahitāni tu  SvaT 
draṣṭavyāni varārohe puruṣādhiṣṭhitāni tu 
sacetanāni sarvāṇi jñātavyāni sadaiva hi  SvaT 
pañcaviṃśakametacca prākṛtaṃ samudāhṛtam 
tato mūrtiṃ nyaseddevi mūlamantrasulakṣitam  SvaT 
sakalaṃ bhairavaṃ nyasya dvātriṃśārṇaṃ sulocane 
mukhāni kalpayetpaścān mūrdhādicaraṇāvadhi  SvaT 
vaktrāṇi kalpayetpaścād ūrdhvaṃ pūrvaṃ ca dakṣiṇam 
uttaraṃ paścimaṃ caiva yathāvatpravibhāgaśaḥ  SvaT 
kalābhedaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ śodhyādhvānaṃ prakalpayet 
navatattvaṃ tritattvaṃ ca vidyāṅgā locanatrayam  SvaT 
vargātītena kṣurikām ūrdhvādho 'gnipradīpitām 
ṣoḍaśāntarhatā sā tu rakṣikā vighnanāśikā  SvaT 
navakaṃ kalpayetpūrvaṃ mūrdhni vaktre ca kaṇṭhake 
hṛdaye nābhideśe ca guhya ūrvośca jānutaḥ  SvaT 
pādāntaṃ caiva vinyasya svadhyānaguṇasaṃyutam 
kriyājñāne tathecchā ca dakṣe vāme ca madhyataḥ  SvaT 
vidyārājaḥ smṛto hyeṣa bhairavo mantranāyakaḥ 
niṣkalaṃ tu tathāvāhya aṅgānyevaṃ yathākramam  SvaT 
gandhairdhūpaistathā puṣpair vividhairbhakṣyabhojanaiḥ 
pūjayeddevadeveśaṃ manasaiva prakalpitaiḥ  SvaT 
ātmānaṃ bhairavaṃ dhyātvā tato hṛdyāgamācaret 
nābhau kandaṃ samāropya nālaṃ tu dvādaśāṅgulam  SvaT 
hṛdantaṃ kalpayedyāvat tatra padmaṃ vicintayet 
aṣṭapatraṃ mahādīptaṃ kesarālaṃ sakarṇikam  SvaT 
kandaṃ śaktimayaṃ tatra nāle vai kaṇṭakāstu ye 
bhuvanāni ca tānyeva rudrāṇāṃ varavarṇini  SvaT 
māyātmako bhavedgranthir aśuddhādhvavyavasthitaḥ 
vidyāpadmaṃ mahādīptaṃ karṇikābījarājitam  SvaT 
puṣkarāṇi ca deveśi tatra vidyeśvarāḥ smṛtāḥ 
evaṃ dhyātvā mahāpadmaṃ sarvadevamayaṃ śubham  SvaT 
śaktinyāso bhavetpūrvaṃ kandaṃ tu tadanantaram 
aṅkuraṃ nālavinyāsam anantaṃ parikalpayet  SvaT 
tejomayaṃ mahāśubhraṃ sphuratkiraṇabhāsvaram 
dharmaṃ jñānaṃ ca vairāgyam aiśvaryaṃ ca kramānnyaset  SvaT 
sitaraktapītakṛṣṇā āgneyyādīśadiggatāḥ 
pādakāḥ siṃharūpāste trinetrā bhīmavikramāḥ  SvaT 
śivaśaktimayā mantrā nyastavyā vīravindate 
adharmājñānāvairāgyam anaiśvaryaṃ ca prāgdiśaḥ  SvaT 
uttarāntaṃ niveśyaṃ tu gātrakāḥ sitavarṇakāḥ 
saṃdhānakīlakāścaiva atasīpuṣpasaṃnibhāḥ  SvaT 
vedā yugāśca te caiva jñātavyāḥ kramaśaḥ priye 
adhaśchādanamūrdhvaṃ ca raktaṃ śuklaṃ vicintayet  SvaT 
madhye tamo vijānīyād guṇāstvete vyavasthitāḥ 
sitaṃ padmaṃ vijānīyāt kesarāṇi vicintayet  SvaT 
sitaraktaprapītāni mūlamadhyāgradeśataḥ 
karṇikā hemasaṃkāśā bījāni haritāni tu  SvaT 
vāmāṃ pūrvadale nyasya jyeṣṭhāṃ vahnidalāśritām 
raudrīṃ dakṣiṇapatre tu kālīṃ nairṛtagocare  SvaT 
kalavikaraṇīṃ devīṃ vinyasyedvāruṇe dale 
balavikaraṇīṃ devīṃ vāyavyadalamāśritām  SvaT 
balapramathanīṃ devīm uttare viniyojayet 
sarvabhūtadamanīṃ ca aiśānyāṃ viniyojayet  SvaT 
madhye manonmanīṃ devīṃ karṇikāyāṃ niveśayet 
śakracāpanibhaṃ devi dhyātavyaṃ śaktimaṇḍalam  SvaT 
madhye sūryasahasrābhāṃ cintayettu manonmanīm 
sūryādhvamaṇḍalaṃ patre somaṃ saṃyojya kesare  SvaT 
vahnimaṇḍalakaṃ devi karṇikāyāṃ niveśayet 
brahmā viṣṇurharaścaiva maṇḍaleṣvadhipāḥ smṛtāḥ  SvaT 
brahmā caturmukho raktaś caturbāhuvibhūṣitaḥ 
kṛṣṇājinottarīyaśca rājīvāsanasaṃsthitaḥ  SvaT 
kamaṇḍaludharo devi daṇḍahastastathaiva ca 
akṣamālādharo devaḥ padmahastaḥ sulocanaḥ  SvaT 
dhyātvā patreṣu taṃ nyasyet sarvakilviṣanāśanam 
atasīpuṣpasaṃkāśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam  SvaT 
pītāmbaradharaṃ devaṃ vanamālāvibhūṣitam 
sphuranmukuṭamāṇikyaṃ kiṅkiṇījālamaṇḍitam  SvaT 
divyakuṇḍaladhartāraṃ garuḍāsanasaṃsthitam 
dhyātvā viṣṇuṃ mahātmānaṃ kesareṣu niveśayet  SvaT 
śaṅkhakundendudhavalaṃ śūlahastaṃ trilocanam 
daśabāhuṃ viśālākṣaṃ nāgayajñopavītinam  SvaT 
siṃhacarmaparīdhānaṃ śaśāṅkakṛtabhūṣaṇam 
nīlakaṇṭhaṃ vṛṣārūḍhaṃ rudraṃ dhyātvā varānane  SvaT 
niveśayetkarṇikāyāṃ mahāpātakanāśanam 
mahāpretaṃ nyasetpaścāt prahasantaṃ sacetanam  SvaT 
raktavarṇaṃ sutejaskaṃ netratrayavibhūṣitam 
praṇavena nyasetsarvam āsanaṃ bhairavasya tu  SvaT 
gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ samabhyarcya tato mūrtiṃ prakalpayet 
kadambakusumākārāṃ tuṣārakiraṇatviṣam  SvaT 
mūrtyūrdhve bhairavaṃ devaṃ sakalaṃ parikalpayet 
dvātriṃśadvarṇakacitaṃ sphurattaḍidivojjvalam  SvaT 
vaktrāṇi kalpayeddevi svadhyānena maheśvari 
mūrdhādicaraṇaṃ yāvat praṇavādinamontataḥ  SvaT 
aṣṭātriṃśatkalābhedaṃ śodhyādhvānaṃ prakalpayet 
navatattvaṃ tritattvaṃ ca navakaṃ bhairavābhidham  SvaT 
vidyāṅgā locanaṃ caiva kṣurikāṃ ca prakalpayet 
śaktitrayaṃ tato nyasyed dakṣadigvāmagocare  SvaT 
madhyapradeśe deveśi tato rūpamanusmaret 
tripañcanayanaṃ devaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitam  SvaT 
candrakoṭipratīkāśāṃ candrārdhakṛtaśekharam 
pañcavaktraṃ viśālākṣaṃ sarpagonāsamaṇḍitam  SvaT 
vṛścikairagnivarṇābhair hāreṇa tu virājitam 
kapālamālābharaṇaṃ khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇam  SvaT 
pāśāṅkuśadharaṃ devaṃ śarahastaṃ pinākinam 
varadābhayahastaṃ ca muṇḍakhaṭvāṅgadhāriṇam  SvaT 
vīṇāḍamaruhastaṃ ca ghaṇṭāhastaṃ triśūlinam 
vajradaṇḍakṛtāṭopaṃ paraśvāyudhahastakam  SvaT 
mudgareṇa vicitreṇa vartulena virājitam 
siṃhacarmaparīdhānaṃ gajacarmottarīyakam  SvaT 
aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ devaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ sutejasam 
ūrdhvavaktraṃ maheśāni sphaṭikābhaṃ vicintayet  SvaT 
āpītaṃ pūrvavaktraṃ tu nīlotpaladalaprabham 
dakṣiṇaṃ tu vijānīyād vāmaṃ caiva vicintayet  SvaT 
dāḍimīkusumaprakhyaṃ kuṅkumodakasaṃnibham 
candrārbudapratīkāśaṃ paścimaṃ tu vicintayet  SvaT 
svacchandabhairavaṃ devaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam 
dhyāyate yastu yuktātmā kṣipraṃ sidhyati mānavaḥ  SvaT 
tataḥ paramabījena paraṃ paramakāraṇam 
suśāntaṃ niṣkalaṃ devaṃ sarvavyāpinirañjanam  SvaT 
āvāhayetsuhṛṣṭātmā tava devi vadāmyaham 
hṛtkaṇṭhatālubhrūmadhya nādāntāntasamāśritam  SvaT 
niṣkampaṃ kāraṇātītam āvāhya parameśvaram 
saṃsthāpya vidhivaddevam aṅgaṣaṭkaṃ tato nyaset  SvaT 
pādyamācamanaṃ cārghaṃ svāgataṃ tadanantaram 
saṃnidhānaṃ ca deveśi niṣṭhurayā nirodhayet  SvaT 
gandhaiḥ puṣpaistathā dhūpair dhūpayitvā tamarcayet 
mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi  SvaT 
tataḥ snānādikaṃ karma kṛtvā caiva varānane 
paridhāpya suvastrāṇi netrapaṭṭodbhavāni ca  SvaT 
vilipyāgurukarpūrair mukuṭādyairvibhūṣayet 
puṣpairnānāvidhaiḥ śubhrair arcayedbhūṣayetpunaḥ  SvaT 
arghaṃ dattvā maheśāni punarmudrāṃ pradarśayet 
praṇamya bhairavaṃ devaṃ svacchandaṃ viśvanāyakam  SvaT 
tato hyābharaṇaṃ bāhye viniveśyaṃ varānane 
aiśānyāṃ pūrvato yāmyāṃ uttarāpyāvasānakam  SvaT 
vinyasetpañca vaktrāṇi pañcavaktrayutāni ca 
bāhubhirdaśabhiścaiva śaśāṅkamukuṭaiḥ saha  SvaT 
dhyātavyāni svarūpāṇi varābhayakarāṇi tu 
agnīśarakṣovāyavya caturdikṣu ca taṃ nyaset  SvaT 
hṛcchiraśca śikhā varma astraṃ ca pravibhāgaśaḥ 
hṛdayaṃ raktavarṇābhaṃ śiro gorocanaprabham  SvaT 
taḍidvalayasaṃkāśāṃ śikhāṃ devīṃ vicintayet 
ādhūmraṃ kavacaṃ vidyāt kapiśaṃ cāstrameva ca  SvaT 
jyotīrūpapratīkāśaṃ netraṃ madhye ca saṃsthitam 
pañcavaktrāḥ smṛtāḥ sarve daśabāhvindubhūṣitāḥ  SvaT 
nānābharaṇasaṃyuktā nānāsraggandhalepanāḥ 
nānāvastraparīdhānā mukuṭairujjvalaiḥ śubhaiḥ  SvaT 
ratnamālāvanaddhāśca hārakeyūrabhūṣitāḥ 
dviraṣṭavarṣakākārāḥ surūpāḥ sthirayauvanāḥ  SvaT 
bhairavādyāḥ smṛtā mantrāḥ pīṭheśāḥ pīṭhamardakāḥ 
yā sā pūrvaṃ mayā khyātā aghorī śaktiruttamā  SvaT 
bhairavaṃ pūjayitvā tu tasyotsaṅge tu tāṃ nyaset 
yādṛśaṃ bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ bhairavyāstādṛgeva hi  SvaT 
īṣatkarālavadanāṃ gambhīravipulasvanām 
prasannāsyāṃ sadā dhyāyed bhairavīṃ vismitekṣaṇām  SvaT 
dvitīyāvaraṇe devi vinyasedbhairavāṣṭakam 
kapālīśaṃ tu pūrvāyām āgneyyāṃ śikhivāhanam  SvaT 
dakṣiṇe krodharājaṃ tu vikarālaṃ tu nairṛte 
manmathaṃ paścime bhāge meghanādeśvaraṃ tathā  SvaT 
vāyavye devi vinyasya somarājaṃ tathottare 
vidyārājaṃ tathaiśānyāṃ vinyasettu subhāvitaḥ  SvaT 
pañcavaktrāstrinetrāśca daśabāhvinduśekharāḥ 
kapālamālābharaṇāḥ sphuranmāṇikyamaṇḍitāḥ  SvaT 
pūrvaṃ pītaṃ smṛtaṃ devi raktamāgreyagocare 
dakṣiṇe nīlameghābhaṃ nairṛtyāṃ jvalanaprabham  SvaT 
śyāmaṃ cāparadigbhāge dhūmraṃ vāyavyagocare 
candrabimbaprabhaṃ saumye īśāne sphaṭikaprabham  SvaT 
tṛtīye caiva lokeśān sāstrānsaṃparikalpayet 
nāmāni teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ  SvaT 
indrāgniyamanirṛti varuṇāśca samīraṇaḥ 
somarājaḥ kuberaśca īśānaḥ parameśvaraḥ  SvaT 
bhairavāṣṭakarūpeṇa dhyātavyāstu varānane 
vajraṃ śaktistathā daṇḍaḥ khaḍgaḥ pāśastathaiva ca  SvaT 
dhvajo gadā triśūlaṃ ca lokapālayudhāni vai 
vajraṃ cānekavarṇāḍhyaṃ śaktiṃ hemasamaprabhām  SvaT 
daṇḍaṃ bhinnāñjanābhaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ nīlotpalaprabham 
kiṃśukābhaṃ tathā pāśaṃ dhvajaṃ śuklaṃ vicintayet  SvaT 
gadāṃ tu vidrumābhāṃ vai śūlaṃ vidyutsamaprabham 
saṃpūjyāvaraṇaṃ sarvaṃ saṃdhānaṃ mantranāyake  SvaT 
astrāṇi lokapālāśca bhairavāṣṭakameva ca 
pañca brahmānyathāṅgāni etānyāvaraṇāni tu  SvaT 
krameṇoccārayetsarvaṃ yāvattadgarbhamaiśvaram 
mūlamantreṇa kartavyaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānameva ca  SvaT 
parāntaṃ yāvadābhāvya naivedyāni nivedayet 
ghārikā vaṭakāṃścaiva śaṣkulīrmodakāṃstathā  SvaT 
khaṇḍalaḍḍuśarāvāṇi bhakṣyāṇi vividhāni ca 
śālyodanaṃ mudgasūpam ājyāktaṃ saṃprakalpayet  SvaT 
kauśalyāṃ maṇḍakāpūpāṃs tathā kṣaudraśirāṃsi ca 
ghṛtāktāṃścillakāṃścaiva lavaṇānparikalpayet  SvaT 
avadaṃśānyanekāni kaṭūni madhurāṇi ca 
rasālāṃ ca dadhi kṣīram āsavaṃ vividhaṃ tathā  SvaT 
matsyamāṃsānyanekāni lehyapeyāni yāni ca 
agramāpūrayecchaṃbhor vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ  SvaT 
paścādarghaḥ pradātavyaḥ surayā susugandhayā 
mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi  SvaT 
praṇipātaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā japaṃ paścātsamācaret 
akṣamālāṃ tu saṃgṛhya gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ samarcitām  SvaT 
vāṅnirudvaḥ sucittātmā rājīvāsanasaṃsthitaḥ 
mūlamantraṃ samuccārya nāde līnaṃ vicintayet  SvaT 
unmīlyākṣāṇi saṃcintya tatastu japamārabhet 
akṣarākṣarasantānaṃ na drutaṃ na vilambitam  SvaT 
japaḥ prāṇasamaḥ kāryaḥ dinastho muktikāṅkṣibhiḥ 
saṃhāraḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ śivadhāmaphalapradaḥ  SvaT 
vyomni prāpto yadā nādaḥ punareva nivartate 
śarvarī sā tu vijñeyā hṛdabjaṃ yāvadāgataḥ  SvaT 
sṛṣṭireṣā samākhyātā sarvasiddhiphalodayā 
ātmano bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ sadā bhāvyaṃ varānane  SvaT 
tasya vighnā vinaśyanti japaśca saphalo bhavet 
japtvā nivedayeddevi bhairavāya varānane  SvaT 
pūrakeṇa prayogeṇa tristhaṃ ca tritayānvitam 
trisiddhisiddhidaṃ devi sarahasyamudāhṛtam  SvaT 
śāntike mānaso japya upāṃśuḥ pauṣṭike smṛtaḥ 
saśabdaścābhicāre 'sau prāgudagdakṣiṇāmukhaḥ  SvaT 
ātmā na śṛṇute yaṃ tu mānaso 'sau prakīrtitaḥ 
ātmanā śrūyate yastu tamupāṃśuṃ vijānate  SvaT 
pare śṛṇvanti yaṃ devi saśabdaḥ sa udāhṛtaḥ 
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva akṣamālā samerukā  SvaT 
rudrākṣaśaṅkhapadmākṣa putrajīvakamauktikaiḥ 
sphāṭikī maṇiratnotthā sauvarṇī vaidrumī tathā  SvaT 
daśākṣamālā deveśi gṛhasthānāṃ prakīrtitāḥ 
sūtraṃ dhyātvā parāṃ śaktim adhvabhāgāṃstato maṇīn  SvaT 
vyaktisthānaṃ śivasyādhvā tatastaddharmiṇīṃ smaret 
saptaviṃśatibhiḥ kuryād dviguṇairvā caturguṇaiḥ  SvaT 
samaistu saṃhatairekaṃ śivatattvātmakaṃ mukhe 
na taṃ vilaṅghayedvidvān sṛṣṭisaṃhārakāraṇam  SvaT 
vīrasthānaratānāṃ hi vīrāṇāṃ varavarṇini 
mahāśaṅkhākṣasūtraṃ tu sarvakāmaphalapradam  SvaT 
gṛhasthena na kartavyam udvegajananaṃ param 
tasmāttu sphāṭikī mālā japtavyā sādhakottamaiḥ  SvaT 
sādhayedvividhānkāmān adhamānmadhyamottamān 
evaṃ hṛdambujāvastho yaṣṭavyo bhairavo vibhuḥ  SvaT 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ kṛtvā paścādyajanamārabhet 
tatrārghapātramādau vai sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tathā  SvaT 
śāṅkhaṃ śāmbūkaṃ śauktaṃ vā tāmraṃ mṛṇmayameva vā 
padmapatrapalāśotthaṃ gṛhītvā kṣālya vāriṇā  SvaT 
astrajaptena deveśi pralipyāgurucandanaiḥ 
mṛṣṭadhūpena saṃdhūpya vāriṇāpūrayettataḥ  SvaT 
vastrapūtena śuddhena tāḍayedastramuccaran 
varmāvaguṇṭhitaṃ kṛtvā yāgaṃ tatraiva vinyaset  SvaT 
pūrvoktena vidhānena prokṣyastena samāsataḥ 
yāgārtho dravyasaṃghātaḥ tato yajanamārabhet  SvaT 
śaktiṃ nyasya tataścādau vyomākārāṃ sujājvalām 
sakalavyāpikāṃ sūkṣmāṃ śivādhārāṃ tu sarvagām  SvaT 
oṃkāradīpitāṃ devīṃ namaskārāvasānikām 
anantaṃ caiva vinyasya dharmaṃ jñānaṃ tathaiva ca  SvaT 
vairāgyaṃ ca tathaiśvaryam āgneyyādikrameṇa tu 
adharmaṃ ca tathājñānam avairāgyamanaiśvaram  SvaT 
saṃdhānakīlakāṃścaiva adhaśchādanamūrdhvagam 
padmaṃ sakesaraṃ devi karṇikāṃ puṣkarāṇi ca  SvaT 
maṇḍalatritayaṃ devāñ śaktīścāpi śivāntakam 
mūrtiṃ brahmakalājālaṃ navatattvaṃ tritattvakam  SvaT 
bhairavāṣṭakavidyāṅga locanaṃ kṣurikāṃ tathā 
śaktitrayaṃ paraṃ devam aṅgaṣaṭkasamanvitam  SvaT 
vinyasya bhāvayeddevi satataṃ vidhipūrvakam 
nirvartya tu yathānyāyaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā  SvaT 
svāgataṃ cārdhyapādyaṃ ca sannidhānaṃ tathaiva ca 
rodhaṃ niṣṭhurayā kuryān mūlamantramanusmaran  SvaT 
pūjā suvipulā kāryā gandhadhūpasragādibhiḥ 
mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścāt tridhā traikālyakarmaṇi  SvaT 
tata āvaraṇaṃ bāhye viniveśyaṃ varānane 
īśapūrvayāmyasaumya varuṇāntaṃ prakalpayet  SvaT 
vaktrāṇāṃ pañcakaṃ devi svadhyānaguṇasaṃyutam 
āgneyaiśānarakṣaḥsu sāmīraindradiśorapi  SvaT 
uttarāntaṃ niveśyaṃ tu aṅgānāṃ pañcakaṃ tathā 
netraṃ tu karṇikāyāṃ vai pūrvasyāṃ diśi saṃsthitam  SvaT 
svamantreṇa tu sarveṣām ardhyaṃ pādyaṃ samāhitaḥ 
mantrasaṃkarapuṣpāṇi na kuryātsādhakaḥ sadā  SvaT 
na bāhuṃ pṛṣṭhato vāpi mantrāṇāṃ parikalpayet 
paripāṭyā tu dātavyaṃ na mantrāṃllaṅghayetkvacit  SvaT 
svamudrāmantrasaṃyuktān yugapatparikalpayet 
ardhyaṃ pādyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca nityaṃ tāvatsamācaret  SvaT 
sarveṣāmeva mantrāṇāṃ vidhireṣa prakīrtitaḥ 
bhairavāṣṭakalokeśān sāstrānsaṃparikalpayet  SvaT 
bāhye śmaśānavinyāsaṃ praṇavādinamontagam 
pūrvādīśānaparyantaṃ kalpayeta vidhānataḥ  SvaT 
āmardakaṃ ca pūrvaṃ vai śmaśānādhipatiṃ vibhum 
śmaśānaiḥ sakabandhaiśca saśūlodbandhabhīṣaṇaiḥ  SvaT 
citibhiḥ prajvalantībhiḥ śivārāvaiḥ subhīṣaṇaiḥ 
agnikaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge kālākhyaṃ paścime tathā  SvaT 
ekapādaṃ tathā saumye āgneyyāṃ tripurāntakam 
nairṛtyāmagnijihvaṃ tu vāyavyāṃ tu karālinam  SvaT 
aiśānyāṃ bhīmavaktraṃ tu śmaśāneśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
tarpayenmatsyamāṃsādyair āsavairvividhaistathā  SvaT 
gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ sarveṣāṃ tu pradāpayet 
praṇipātaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā japtvā mantraṃ subhāvitaḥ  SvaT 
recakena prayogena nivedya vidhipūrvakam 
huḍḍuṅkāranamaskārān kṛtvā caiva tato vrajet  SvaT 
agnikuṇḍasamīpaṃ tu arghahastaḥ subhāvitaḥ 
kuṇḍaṃ tu lakṣaṇopetaṃ prokṣayedastravāriṇā  SvaT 
kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaitad astradarbheṇa collikhet 
uddhṛtya prokṣayetpaścād astramantreṇa bhāmini  SvaT 
pūraṇaṃ tena kartavyaṃ samīkaraṇameva ca 
secanaṃ kuṭṭanaṃ caiva lepanaṃ tena kārayet  SvaT 
prokṣaṇaṃ śoṣaṇaṃ caiva tathāstreṇaiva kārayet 
pūjanaṃ gandhapuṣpādyaiḥ asinā cābhimantraṇam  SvaT 
vajrīkaraṇamastreṇa rekhāḥ pūrvāparāstrayaḥ 
yāmyasaumyamukhī caikā vajrametatprakīrtitam  SvaT

śivapūjāgnikāryādau sakalīkṛtavigrahaḥ  SvaT 
nānyathā prāksvarūpeṇa pūjanārho bhavettu saḥ 
nītvā kuṇḍasamīpaṃ taṃ śiṣyahastāviyogataḥ  SvaT 
ātmasavye 'tha digbhāge maṇḍalaṃ praṇavena tu 
praṇavenāsanaṃ dattvā tasyopari śiśuṃ nyaset  SvaT 
upaveśya kare darbhaṃ bhairaveṇa samarpayet 
mūlaṃ śiṣyasya hastasthaṃ sāgramācāryajaṅghayoḥ  SvaT 
piṅgalā madhyamā nāḍī śiṣyadehādvinirgatā 
saivātra darbhabhūtā tu gurunāḍyāṃ layaṃ gatā  SvaT 
nāḍīsandhānahetvarthaṃ bhairaveṇāhutitrayam 
tayā nāḍyā praveṣṭavyaṃ śiṣyasya hṛdaye sakṛt  SvaT 
grahaṇākarṣaṇārthaṃ tu gṛhṇan muñcan punaḥ punaḥ 
dīkṣākāle yataścaivaṃ tadarthaṃ nāḍisaṃhatiḥ  SvaT 
śiṣyasyātha śirobhūmau bhairaveṇa vidhāya tu 
sampātaṃ sarvamantraistu dhruveṇājyāhutiṃ kṣipet  SvaT 
mūlamantraṃ samuccārya svā ityagnau prapātayet 
heti śiṣyasya śirasi sampātaḥ śivacoditaḥ  SvaT 
śiṣyadehe tu ye mantrāḥ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ sthitāḥ 
kuṇḍasthāḥ pūjitā ye tu dhāmādyāvaraṇāntagāḥ  SvaT 
yugapattarpaṇaṃ teṣāṃ sampātastena kīrtitaḥ 
ekaikasyātra mantrasya āhutitritayena tu  SvaT 
utthāpya ca tataḥ śiṣyaṃ tadarthaṃ mantratarpaṇam 
bhairavāya śataṃ hutvā hṛdādau daśakaṃ hutiḥ  SvaT 
dhāmnā cotthāya hotavyaṃ pūrṇāhutyānutarpayet 
mantrāṇāṃ dīpanaṃ kuryād dhāmādyastrāvadhi kramāt  SvaT 
huṃkāradvayamadhye tu mūlamantraṃ samuccaran 
praṇavādiphaḍantena āhutīḥ pratipādayet  SvaT 
hṛdādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ jātiruktātra dīpane 
pāśānāṃ bandhanārthāya mantrāṇāṃ dīpanaṃ smṛtam  SvaT 
mantrāḥ karaṇabhūtāstu paśukāryasya sādhane 
ācāryaḥ karaṇaṃ proktaḥ śivarūpo yataḥ smṛtaḥ  SvaT 
krūrakārye tu kartavye mantrān sandīpya yojayet 
krūrajātyanurūpeṇa vācakān yojayet sadā  SvaT 
bhrukuṭīkarālavadanān vācyarūpān vicintayet 
saumyajātiyutān saumye saumyarūpān vicintayet  SvaT 
pāśakarma tato vakṣye kanyākartitasūtrakam 
triguṇaṃ triguṇīkṛtya pāśabandhanasūtrakam  SvaT 
śivāmbho 'streṇa samprokṣya kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
pūjayitvā vidhānena gandhapuṣpādidhūpakaiḥ  SvaT 
prasārayedgṛhītvā tan mūrdhādyaṅguṣṭhakāvadhi 
śiṣyasya stabdhadehasya nāḍībhūtaṃ vicintayet  SvaT 
suṣumnā madhyamā nāḍī sarvanāḍīsamanvitā 
oṃkārādi svanāmnā tu namaskārāvasānakam  SvaT 
śiṣyadehasthitāṃ nāḍīṃ sūtre saṃgṛhya yojayet 
gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjya kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet  SvaT 
sannidhānāhutīstisraḥ svanāmapadajātikāḥ 
śivāmbho 'streṇa samprokṣya śiṣyasya hṛdayaṃ punaḥ  SvaT 
tāḍayedastrapuṣpeṇa hṛdi citsaṃhṛtā bhavet 
huṃkāroccārayogena recakena viśeddhṛdi  SvaT 
nāḍīrandhreṇa gatvā tu caitanyaṃ bhāvayecchiṣoḥ 
kadambagolakākāraṃ sphurattārakasannibham  SvaT 
hṛtsthaṃ chittvāstrakhaḍgena humphaṭkārāntajātinā 
dhāmnā cāṅkuśarūpeṇa karṣecchaktyavadhi kramāt  SvaT 
dvādaśāntaṃ tu saṃgṛhya sampuṭya hṛdayena tu 
saṃhāramudrayā yojyaṃ sūtre nāḍīprakalpite  SvaT 
vyāpakaṃ bhāvayitvā tu kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
bhairaveṇāhutīstisraḥ sannidhānasya hetave  SvaT 
dvitīyaḥ sūtradehastu pāśā yatra sthitāstvime 
bandyāścedyāstathā dāhyāḥ sūtrasthāne na vigrahe  SvaT 
pāśāstu trividhā bhāvyā māyīyāṇavakarmajāḥ 
caitanyarodhakāstvete kāryakāraṇarūpiṇaḥ  SvaT 
malaḥ karma nimittaṃ tu naimittikamataḥ param 
ādhārarūpaṃ naimittaṃ śarīrabhuvanādikam  SvaT 
nimittamabhilāṣākhyaṃ vicitrairheturūpakaiḥ 
tāṃścāvalokayet sūtre bandhyabandhanahetutaḥ  SvaT 
pāśānāṃ tāḍanaṃ kāryaṃ humphaṭkārāntajātinā 
svanāmapraṇavādyena śāntyatītādyanukramāt  SvaT 
puṣpeṇa tāḍayenmūrdhni grāhyaṃ hūmādi yojayet 
huṃphakārāntayogenā gṛhya saṃhāramudrayā  SvaT 
dhāmnā tu yojayet sūtre namaskārāntayoginā 
evaṃ śāntyādikān pāśān sthānāt saṃgṛhya yojayet  SvaT 
bhāvayettrividhān pāśān pañcatattvādhvavyāpakān 
trayāṇāṃ vyāpikā śaktiḥ kriyākhyā pārameśvarī  SvaT 
śāntyatītādibhedena pañcasaṃjñāpratiṣṭhitā 
ādheyagraha ādhāraṃ gṛhītaṃ bhāvayet paśoḥ  SvaT 
gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ pūjya sūtre pāśāṃśtu tarpayet 
śāntyatītākrameṇaiva āhutīnāṃ trayaṃ trayam  SvaT 
sannidhānāya pāśānām ataḥ pāśāṃstu dīpayet 
svanāmajātiphaṭkāra dhāmabhiśca trayaṃ trayam  SvaT 
viśleṣakaraṇārthaṃ tu pāśānāṃ dīpanaṃ bhavet 
dīptāḥ pāśāstato bandhyās tāḍanagrahaṇādinā  SvaT 
sūtrasthāṃstāḍayetpuṣpaiḥ svadehasthāniva kramāt 
dhāmnā ca sampuṭīkṛtya svanāmnā ca sakṛtsakṛt  SvaT 
bandhane tu prayogo 'yaṃ sūtre granthīn pradāpayet 
bandhane parimāṇaṃ ca karmaṇo viṣayasya ca  SvaT 
ṣaṭtriṃśattattvamadhyastho bhuṅkte bhogaṃ na cānyathā 
pāśān saṃsthāpya pātre tu saṃpātaṃ juhuyāt sakṛt  SvaT 
pātrasampuṭamadhyasthān sthaṇḍile vinivedayet 
nītvā samarpayet kumbhe pāśān saṃrakṣa he vibho  SvaT 
darbhaṃ vimocayecchiṣyaṃ puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradāpayet 
shtaṇḍile śivakumbhe ca śivāgnau ca prapūjayet  SvaT 
tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā daṇḍavannipatedbhuvi 
utthāpya pañcagavyādīn dadyādvai bhairaveṇa tu  SvaT 
gomayena śucau deśe kāryaṃ maṇḍalakatrayam 
ekasmin maṇḍale viṣṭaḥ pañcagavyaṃ śiśuḥ pibet  SvaT 
upaviśya dvitīye tu carukaṃ prāśayedbudhaḥ 
ācamya dantakāṣṭhaṃ tu tṛtīye maṇḍale sthitaḥ  SvaT 
bhakṣayitvā ca deveśi tataścaiva vinikṣipet 
pūrvaṃ paścāttathaiśordhvaṃ cottarasyāṃ ca śobhanam  SvaT 
anyasyāmaśubhaṃ viddhi tasya homaḥ śataṃ bhavet 
ācāryo juhuyāt paścāt prāyaścittaṃ śivena tu  SvaT 
vidhernyūnātiriktasya cittavikṣepakarmaṇi 
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā prāyaścittād viśuddhyati  SvaT 
paścātsantarpayeddhoma sahasreṇa śatena vā 
mantrāṃśca daśabhāgena vahnau naivedyadāpanam  SvaT 
viśeṣapūjanaṃ cārghaṃ mudrābandhaṃ varānane 
stotraṃ vādyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā caruṃ prāśya visarjayet  SvaT 
nirodhārgheṇa cārghaṃ tu dattvā caiva varānane 
recakena tu saṃgṛhya bhairavaṃ tamanusmaran  SvaT 
muṣṭinā pūritaṃ nītvā pūjayitvā varānane 
agniṣṭhaṃ vai pūrakeṇa gṛhītvā sthāpayet punaḥ  SvaT 
tatrasthaṃ pūjayitvā ca kalaśe tu vinikṣipet 
kusumādibhirabhyarcya kumbha eva tu bhairavam  SvaT 
prakṣipya caiva nirmālyaṃ gomayena spṛśet priye 
śivāmbhasā tu samprokṣya śiṣye śayyāṃ prakalpayet  SvaT 
gṛhiṇo darbhaśayyāṃ tu yatervai bhasmanā priye 
pūrvāśirā gṛhī kāryo yatirvai dakṣiṇāśirāḥ  SvaT 
tatra sthitasya śiṣyasya śikhābandhaṃ varānane 
siddhārtharocanādyaiśca rakṣāṃ kuryādasiṃ smaran  SvaT 
bhasmanā rocanādyaiśca astraprākāracintanam 
kavacenāvaguṇṭhyaiva śiṣyaṃ tu svāpayettataḥ  SvaT 
tataścaiva tu nirgatya balikarma samārabhet 
balistu kalpitaḥ pūrvaṃ sarvabhūteṣvathādarāt  SvaT 
taṃ tu saṃgṛhya deveśi pūrvādīśāntakaṃ kṣipet 
bhūtā ye vividhākārā divyabhaumāntarikṣagāḥ  SvaT 
pātālatalasaṃsthāśca śivayāge subhāvitāḥ 
dhruvādisarvabhūtāśca aindrādyāśāsthitāśca ye  SvaT 
svāhākārasamāyogāt tṛpyantūccārayan kṣipet 
namaskāreṇa sampūjya gandhairdhūpairanukramāt  SvaT 
pūrvādīśānaparyantam adhaścordhvaṃ samantataḥ 
koṇasthān kṣetrapālāṃśca patitāñchvapacānapi  SvaT 
baliṃ dattvā tu sarvebhya ācamya ca varānane 
sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā krameṇa prāśayeccarum  SvaT 
sahāyaiḥ sahito vīra ekacittaḥ samāhitaḥ 
prāṅmukha udaṅmukho vā maṇḍalasthaḥ pṛthakpṛthak  SvaT 
pañcagavyaṃ pibet pūrvaṃ carukaṃ dantadhāvanam 
prāśyaivaṃ sakalīkṛtya rakṣāṃ pūrvavadeva ca  SvaT 
yāgabūmau svapet pāścāc chiṣyaiḥ saha varānane 
bhairavadhyānayogena samādhau jāgradeva vā  SvaT 
svacchandatantre 'dhivāsapaṭalastṛtīyaḥ
caturthaḥ paṭalaḥ
adhivāsānantarabhāvinīṃ dīkṣāṃ prastāvayituṃ śrībhairava uvāca
pratyūṣe vimale kṛtvā śaucādyān purrvavatkramāt 
sakalīkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā pūrvavat praviśedgṛham  SvaT 
śiṣyaśca śucirācāntaḥ puṣpahastaḥ 
guruṃ tataḥ 
praṇamya śirasā 
hṛṣṭo guroḥ svapnānnivedayet  SvaT 
śubhān svapnān pravakṣyāmi aśubhāṃśca varānane 
svapneṣu madirāpānam āmamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇam  SvaT 
krimiviṣṭhānulepaṃ ca rudhireṇābhiṣecanam 
bhakṣaṇaṃ dadhibhaktasya śvetavastrānulepanam  SvaT 
śvetātapatraṃ mūrdhasthaṃ śvetasragdāma bhūṣaṇam 
siṃhāsanaṃ rathaṃ yānaṃ dhvajaṃ rājyābhiṣecanam  SvaT 
ratnāṅgābharaṇādīni tāmbūlaṃ phalameva ca 
darśanaṃ śrīsarasvatyoḥ śubhanāryavagūhanam  SvaT 
narendrairṛṣibhirdevaiḥ siddhavidyādharairgaṇaiḥ 
ācāryaiḥ saha saṃvādaṃ kṛtvā svapne prasiddhyati  SvaT 
nadīsamudrataraṇam ākāśagamanaṃ tathā 
bhāskarodayanaṃ caiva prajvalantaṃ hutāśanam  SvaT 
grahanakṣatratārāṇāṃ candrabimbasya darśanam 
harmyasyārohaṇaṃ caiva prāsādaśikhare 'pi vā  SvaT 
narāśvavṛṣapotebha taruśailāgrarohaṇam 
vimānagamanaṃ caiva siddhamantrasya darśanam  SvaT 
lābhaḥ siddhacaroścaiva devādīnāṃ ca darśanam 
guṭikāṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca khaḍgapādukarocanāḥ  SvaT 
upvītāñjanaṃ caiva amṛtaṃ pāratauṣadhīḥ 
śaktiṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ padmam akṣasūtraṃ manaḥśilām  SvaT 
prajvalatsiddhadravyāṇi gairikāntāni yāni ca 
dṛṣṭvā siddhyati svapnānte kṣitilābhaṃ vraṇaṃ tathā  SvaT 
kṣatajārṇavasāṃgrāma taraṇaṃ vijayaṃ raṇe 
jvalatpitṛvanaṃ ramyaṃ vīravīreśibhirvṛtam  SvaT 
vīravetālasiddhaiśca mahāmāṃsasya vikrayam 
mahāpāśoḥ saṃvibhāgaṃ labdhvā devebhya ādarāt  SvaT 
ātmanā pūjayan devaṃ japan dhyāyan stuvannapi 
suhutaṃ cānalaṃ dīptaṃ pūjitaṃ vā prapaśyati  SvaT 
haṃsasārasacakrāhva mayūraśavarohaṇam 
mātṛbhirbhairavaścaiva mātṛrudragaṇaiḥ saha  SvaT 
bhairavaṃ bhairavīṃ dṛṣṭvā siddhyatyatra na saṃśayaḥ 
śubhāḥ svapnā mayākhyātā aśubhāṃśca nibodha me  SvaT 
tailābhyaṅgastathā pānaṃ viśanaṃ ca rasātale 
andhakūpe ca patanam atha paṅke nimajjanam  SvaT 
vṛkṣavāhanayānebhyaḥ patanaṃ harmyaparvatāt 
kartanaṃ karṇanāsābhyām atha vā hastapādayoḥ  SvaT 
patanaṃ dantakośānām ṛkṣavānaradarśanam 
vetālakrūrasatvānāṃ tathaiva kālapūruṣāḥ  SvaT 
kṛṣṇordhvakeśā malināḥ kṛṣṇamālyāmbaracchadāḥ 
raktākṣī strī ca yaṃ svapne puruṣaṃ tvavagūhayet  SvaT 
mriyate nātra saṃdeho yadi śāntiṃ na kārayet 
gṛhaprasādabhedaṃ ca śayyāvastrāsaneṣu ca  SvaT 
ātmano 'bhibhavaṃ saṃkhya ātmadravyāpahāraṇam 
kharoṣṭraśvasṛgāleṣu kaṅkagṛdhrabakeṣu ca  SvaT 
mahiṣolūkakākeṣu rohaṇam ca pravartanam 
bhakṣaṇam pakvamāṃsasya raktamālyānulepanam  SvaT 
kṛṣṇaraktāni vastrāṇi vikṛtātmā prapaśyati 
hasanaṃ valganaṃ svapne mlānasragdāmadhāraṇam  SvaT 
svamāṃsotkartanaṃ bandhaṃ kṛṣṇasarpeṇa bhakṣaṇam 
udvāhaṃ ca tathā svapne dṛṣṭvā naiva prasidhyati  SvaT 
aśubhā hyevamākhyātā vijñeyā deśikottamaiḥ 
śubhāstatrānumedyāstu aśubheṣu tu homayet  SvaT 
aṣṭottaraśataṃ dhāmnā prāyaścittādviśuddhyati 
pūrvavat sakalīkṛtya vighnoccāṭanarakṣaṇam  SvaT 
veṣṭanaṃ pūrvavat kuryāc chivambhaḥ śivahastakam 
lokapālāṃstu saṃpūjya śivakumbhaṃ ca sthaṇḍilam  SvaT 
agnikāryaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ pūrṇāhutiprapātanam 
prāyaścittaṃ tataḥ paścād dusvapnārthaṃ yaduktavān  SvaT 
evaṃ pūjādikaṃ kṛtvā visṛjya sthaṇḍilacchivam 
nirmālyāpanayaṃ kṛtvā bhūmiṃ saṃśodhya pūrvavat  SvaT 
nityakarma tataḥ kuryāt pūjāhomajapādikam 
nityāhnike samāpte tu naimittikamathācaret  SvaT 
upalipya śivāmbhobhir bramhmasthānaṃ prapūjayet 
bhāvena gandhapuṣpādyaiḥ tato maṇḍalamālikhet  SvaT 
karaṇīṃ khaṭikāṃ caiva bhairaveṇa prapūjayet 
dhāmnā tu rajasāṃ pātaḥ sitādyaśvāgamoditaḥ  SvaT 
niṣpanne maṇḍale snātvā nityakarma samācaret 
nityakarmasamāptau tu kuryānnaimittikaṃ budhaḥ  SvaT 
snānādi pūrvamantraiḥ sakalīkaraṇādikam 
ātmarakṣāstraprākāra dvārapālādipūjanam  SvaT 
vighnoccāṭanadigbandhau bhūpātālakhavāsinām 
astraprākāramāropya kavacenāvaguṇṭhanam  SvaT 
udaṅmukhaṃ tūpaviṣṭaḥ karaśuddhyādi pūrvavat 
śivāmbhaḥ śivahastaṃ ca arghatrayaprakalpanam  SvaT 
lokapālāṃstu saṃpūjya śivakumbhaṃ prapūjayet 
maṇḍalasyāgrato bhūtvā maṇḍalaṃ prokṣya cāsinā  SvaT 
varmaṇā veṣṭayet paścāt praṇavenābhimantrayet 
aṣṭottaraśataṃ dhāmnā rajodoṣairviśuddhyati  SvaT 
caturdikṣvastraṃ saṃpūjya dvāre gandhādibhiḥ kramāt 
prākāraṃ bhāvayedastraṃ maṇḍalaṃ praviśet tataḥ  SvaT 
gurūn saṃpūjya vighneśaṃ puṣpādyaiḥ praṇavena tu 
anantamāsanaṃ prāgvac chivāntaṃ praṇavena tu  SvaT 
mūrtyādi pūrvannyasyed dhṛdādyāvaraṇāntagam 
pūrvoktavidhinā pūjya naivedyāni nivedayet  SvaT 
nirodhārgheṇa cārdhaṃ tu datvā caiva nirodhayet 
japadhyānādikaṃ kṛtvā agniṣṭhaṃ bhairavaṃ yajet  SvaT 
nāḍīsaṃdhānakaṃ triṣṭhaṃ kṛtvā saṃtarpayedvibhum 
ātmano niṣkaloccāraṃ kṛtvā kumbhe niveśayet  SvaT 
kalaśasthasya vāmena rocayet pūrayettataḥ 
maṇḍalasthasya savyena punarvāmena rocayet  SvaT 
agniṣṭhasya tu tattejo dakṣiṇena viśan smaret 
evaṃ sādhanakaṃ kṛtvā tatastarpaṇamārabhet  SvaT 
daśabhāgavibhāgena hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet 
prāyaścittaviśuddhyarthaṃ kuryādaṣṭottaraṃ śatam  SvaT 
vidheḥ pūrṇātiriktasya dhāmnā pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ 
ācāryoṭhārdhahastastu maṇḍalaṃ praviśettataḥ  SvaT 
saṃpūjya parameśānaṃ puṣpādyairardhapaścimam 
mudrāṃ baddhvā praṇamyādau jānubhyāmavaniṃ gataḥ  SvaT 
vijñāpayeta paśvarthaṃ prārabdhyoyaṃ makhottamaḥ 
snānādhivāsanādyaṃ yan maṇḍale 'gnau ca yatkṛtam  SvaT 
vidhānaṃ puṣkalaṃ samyak tvatprasādādihāstu tat 
idānīṃ śiṣyadehe tu sakalīkaraṇādikā  SvaT 
yojanyantādhvaśuddhistu tvatprasādāt prasiddhyatu 
evamastvityanujñātaḥ parameśena vīrarāṭ  SvaT 
labdhānujñaḥ prahṛṣṭātmā niṣkrāmenmaṇḍalādbahiḥ 
paśvarthāya kṛtaṃ yattu tadgṛhītvārdhapātrakam  SvaT 
dhāmnastu dakṣiṇe bhāge kārayenmaṇḍalaṃ guruḥ 
praṇavāsanaṃ kuśairnyasya śuciṃ śiṣyaṃ niveśayet  SvaT 
śivāmbho 'streṇa saṃtāḍya bhasmanā ca kuśaiḥ kramāt 
maṇḍale kalpite śiṣyaṃ mūrtibhūtaṃ prakalpayet  SvaT 
upaviśya karanyāsaṃ nirdāhādyastrapūrvakam 
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ nyāsaṃ mantrasaṃdhānameva ca  SvaT 
śivahastaḥ pradātavyo dhyātvā devaṃ sujājvalam 
mūrdhni saṃpātayettejaḥ pāśāṅkuravināśanam  SvaT 
utthāpya ca tato nītvā maṇḍalaṃ tu praveśayet 
vastraṃ saṃprokṣya toyena kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet  SvaT 
pūjayedgandhapuṣpādyair bhairaveṇābhimantrayet 
netre baddhā tu netreṇa puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradāpayet  SvaT 
akāmānnikṣipetpuṣpaṃ devasyābhimukhaṃ sthitaḥ 
puṣpapātavaśānnāma kuryādvai sādhakasya ca  SvaT 
mumukṣorgururicchātaḥ nāma vai sādhakasya vā 
mukhamudghāṭya taṃ śiṣyaṃ śivāya praṇipātayet  SvaT 
pradakṣiṇamataḥ kṛtvā maṇḍalegnau praṇamya ca 
agnikuṇḍasamīpe tu ācāryaḥ paśunā saha  SvaT 
ātmasavyetha digbhāge maṇḍalaṃ praṇavena tu 
pūrvannāḍisaṃdhānaṃ tad arthaṃ cāhutitrayam  SvaT 
saṃpātābhihutiṃ kṛtvā aṇutarpaṇameva ca 
pūrṇāhutiṃ tato dattvā prāyaścittāni homayet  SvaT 
dhāmnā cāṣṭaśataṃ paścāt pātayedāhutitrayam 
jātyuddhāre dhruveṇaiva dvijatvāpādane tathā  SvaT 
bījāhāre tathā deśa bhāvaśuddhau dvijo bhavet 
praṇavenāhutīstisro rudrāṃśāpādane tathā  SvaT 
astreṇa prokṣayecchiṣyaṃ puṣpayuktena tāḍayet 
recakena tato gatvā śiṣyadehe viśeddhṛdi  SvaT 
oṃkārādi śivaṃ japtvā astramantraṃ phaḍantagam 
viśleṣakaraṇaṃ kṛtvā caitanyasya vidhānataḥ  SvaT 
chedayedastramantreṇa kavacenāvaguṇṭhayet 
aṅkuśena samākṛṣya dvādaśānte tu kārayet  SvaT 
tatrasthaḥ pudgalo grāhyaḥ saṃpuṭyaiva dhruveṇa tu 
saṃhāramudrayā samyak pūrakeṇa viśeddhṛdi  SvaT 
saṃskubhya sarasīkṛtya recayetpudgalaṃ punaḥ 
tyajantaṃ devatāṣaṭkaṃ tataścāpi svakaṃ padam  SvaT 
tatrasthaṃ pudgalaṃ gṛhya saṃpuṭya ca bhavena tu 
saṃhāramudrayoddhṛtya śiṣyasya hṛdi yojayet  SvaT 
bhairaveṇābhimantrya evam upavītaṃ śiśordadet 
ādhānādyāvadantyeṣṭiṃ dvijatve saṃskṛto bhavet  SvaT 
piṇḍasyāpādanaṃ jāteḥ āhutitritayena tu 
caitanyasyāpi saṃskāram ādhānāntyeṣṭitaḥ param  SvaT 
sūkṣmavijñānataḥ kṛtvā dvijatve saṃskṛto bhavet 
śatahomaṃ sahasraṃ vā hutvā pūrṇāhutiṃ tataḥ  SvaT 
samayī saṃskṛto hyevaṃ vacaneṣyārhatā bhavet 
śravaṇe 'dhyayane home pūjanādau tathaiva ca  SvaT 
caryādhyānaviśuddhātmā labhate padamaiśvaram 
atha dīkṣādhvaśuddhyarthaṃ bhuktimuktiphalārthinām  SvaT 
vidhānamucyate sūkṣmaṃ pāśavicchattikārakam 
guruḥ saṃpṛcchate śiṣyaṃ dvividhaṃ phalakāṅkṣiṇam  SvaT 
phalamākāṅkṣase yādṛk tādṛk sādhanamārabhe 
vāsanābhedataḥ prāptiḥ sādhyamantrapracoditā  SvaT 
mantramudrādhvadravyāṇāṃ homaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
vāsanābhedato bhinnaḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ ca gurostathā  SvaT 
sādhako dvividhastatra śivadharmyekataḥ sthitaḥ 
śivamantraviśuddhādhvā sādhyamantraniyojitaḥ  SvaT 
jñānavāṃścābhiṣiktaśca mantrārādhanatatparaḥ 
trividhāyāstu siddhervai so 'trārhaḥ śivasādhakaḥ  SvaT 
dvitīyo lokamārgastha iṣṭāpūrtavidhau rataḥ 
karmakṛtphalamākāṅkṣañ śubhaikastho 'śubhojjhitaḥ  SvaT 
tasya kāryaṃ sadā mantrair aśubhāṃśavināśanam 
gṛhastho vā yatirvāsāv āśramaikatamasthitaḥ  SvaT 
mumukṣurdvividhaḥ prokto nirbījo bījavānpunaḥ 
bālabāliśavṛddhastrī bhogabhugvyādhitātmanām  SvaT 
eṣāṃ nirbījikā dīkṣā samayadivivarjitā 
vidvaddvandvasahānā tu sabījā kīrtitā priye  SvaT 
dīkṣānugrāhikā teṣāṃ samayācārasaṃyutā 
viśeṣasamayācārā mantrākhye ye prakīrtitāḥ  SvaT 
te 'tra pālyāḥ prayatnena mokṣasiddhimabhīpsatā 
sabījā sā tuvijñeyā putrakācāryayoḥ sthitā  SvaT 
gṛhastho vāśramī vātha yatiḥ saṃkalpya dīkṣayet 
pāśasūtrakamādāya śiṣyadehe 'valambayet  SvaT 
adhvānaṃ saṃdhayedagnau dhāmnā caiva vicakṣaṇaḥ 
kumbhamaṇḍalavahnisthaś cādhvātmasthaḥ śiśośca yaḥ  SvaT 
sūtrasthaścāpi caikatra adhvasaṃdhiḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
ṣaḍvidhasyādhvamārgasya sādhāraṇagatasya tu  SvaT 
kuṇḍe saṃkalpya saṃśodhya madhvasaṃdhau tu homayet 
mūlamantrāṣṭaśatika madhvasaṃdhānahetutaḥ  SvaT 
adhvāvalokanaṃ paścād vyāpyavyāpakabhedataḥ 
bhuvanavyāptitā tattveṣv anantādiśivāntake  SvaT 
vyāpakāni ca ṣaṭtriṃśat mantravarṇapadātmakāḥ 
tattvāntarbhāvinaḥ sarve vācyavācakayogataḥ  SvaT 
kalāntarbhāvinaste vai nivṛttyādyāśca tāḥ smṛtāḥ 
hṛdādyā vācakāstāsāṃ bījāmantrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  SvaT 
ekikasyāḥ kalāyāśca pṛthagvyāptiṃ vibhāvayet 
pṛthivyādikalā jñeyā brahmādyāḥ kāraṇāśca te  SvaT 
evaṃ vyāptiṃ bhāvayitvā adhvopasthāpanaṃ bhavet 
trirāhutiṃ dhruveṇaiva adhvaśuddhirato bhavet  SvaT 
agnau tu pūjite deve adhvanyāse kṛte sati 
tadeva pādādārabhya pṛthivyādikramānnyaset  SvaT 
dhāmādhiḥ praṇavādiśca nivṛttyai ca namaḥ punaḥ 
upasthāpanamantro 'yaṃ vyāptiṃ dhyātvādhvasaṃsthitām  SvaT 
nivṛttyabhyantare pṛthvī śatakoṭipravistarā 
tasyāṃ ca bhuvanānāṃ ca śatamaṣṭottarāvadhi  SvaT 
aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ padāni varṇa eko 'tra saṃsthitaḥ 
mantrau dvāveva vijñeyau adhvaṣaṭkaṃ vibhāvayet  SvaT 
puṣpagandhādinā pūjya saṃnidhāvāhutitrayam 
māyīyā bhuvanākārā malāḥ karma ca saṃsthitāḥ  SvaT 
śarīrabhuvanākārā māyīyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
bhogahetuśca karma syād abhilāṣo malo 'tra tu  SvaT 
evaṃ pāśatrayaṃ bhāvyaṃ dīkṣāyāmadhvasaṃsthitam 
tadviśuddhyai ca dīkṣā ca kriyate sā yathāvidhi  SvaT 
ādau śaktiṃ nyaseddevi kalātattvasamanvitām 
hṛdā saṃkalpya vāgīśīṃ vyāpikāṃ sarvayoniṣu  SvaT 
śatarudrādyanantāntaṃ yonayo vividhāḥ sthitāḥ 
samakālamṛtutvena vāgīśīṃ saṃnidhāpayet  SvaT 
dhruveṇa pūjayetpuṣpair gandhadhūpairanukramāt 
oṃkāreṇāhutistisro vāgīśīsaṃnidhāpane  SvaT 
śiṣyaṃ saṃprokṣya cāstreṇa tāḍayedastramuccaran 
recakenātmano gatvā chindyāttasyāsinā hṛdaḥ  SvaT 
dhāmnākṛṣya tadātmānaṃ dvādaśānte nidhāpayet 
dhruveṇa tatsthaṃ saṃpuṭya caitanyaṃ mudrayātmani  SvaT 
pūrayedbhairaveṇaiva kumbhayedrecayettataḥ 
dvādaśāntāttu saṃgṛhya yojayedbhavamudrayā  SvaT 
ātmānamīśvaraṃ dhyātvā māyāṃ vāgīśvarīmapi 
saṃyojya tasyāṃ caitanyaṃ śarīrāṇyadhvani sṛjet  SvaT 
prākkarmavāsanāśeṣa phalabhogatvahetave 
yugapadbhinnabhogāni deśakālaśarīrataḥ  SvaT 
mantraśaktyā vipacyante pudgalāśca tathāvidhāḥ 
bhinādehā visṛjyante garbhe vāgīśiyoniṣu  SvaT 
dhāmnā ca yojayitvā ca juhuyādāhutitrayam 
yugapatsarvagarbheṣu dehā vividharūpakāḥ  SvaT 
bhairavecchāsusaṃpannaḥ śatarudrādyanantagāḥ 
garbheṣu garbhaniṣpatti bhairaveṇāhutitrayam  SvaT 
hutvā tu jananaṃ kāryaṃ punastenāhutitrayāt 
sarvayoniṣu dehāste yugapadvṛddhimāgatāḥ  SvaT 
bhoganiṣpattaye karma vyāparasahakāraṇam 
tadabhāvānna bhogaḥ syāt tadarthaṃ mārjanaṃ smṛtam  SvaT 
arjite ārjite sati bhoktavyo bhogo duḥkhasukhātmakaḥ 
layaḥ paramayā prītyā sukhaduḥkhādike 'pyalam  SvaT 
tisṛbhistisṛbhirhomaṃ dhāmnaiva triṣu kārayet 
āhutīnāṃ śataṃ homyaṃ dhāmnā niṣkṛtaye punaḥ  SvaT 
yatkarmabhogyarūpaṃ tu jātyāyurbhogalakṣaṇam 
niṣkṛtyante viśuddhyettad bhūlokasamavasthitam  SvaT 
saṃsārā daśacatvāraḥ saṃskārā aṣṭabhiḥ saha 
catvāriṃśad dvijatvāya vakṣyante bhuvanādhvani  SvaT 
yonirbījaṃ tathā bhāva āhāro deśa eva ca 
eteṣāṃ śodhanaṃ devi rudrāṃśāpādanaṃ tathā  SvaT 
atrāvalokanaṃ kṛtvā niṣkṛtyāmeva śuddhyati 
viṣayā bhuvanākārā ye kecidbhogyarūpiṇaḥ  SvaT 
bhuktakarmaphalāśeṣā niṣkṛtistena sā smṛtā 
viśleṣo niṣkṛterbhogāt bhogābhāve sa hi smṛtaḥ  SvaT 
bhoktṛtvaṃ viṣayāsaktir malakāryaṃ prakīrtitam 
bhoktṛtvābhāvastatraiva śarīreṇa tu yatkṛtam  SvaT 
viśleṣaḥ kriyate tasya paśormantraiḥ śivājñayā 
dhāmnā cāhutayastisro viśleṣakaraṇāya ca  SvaT 
āhutitritayaṃ dhāmnā pāśacchede 'pi dāpayet 
pāśā dehe tu māyīyāḥ kalādyā bhūtakāvadhi  SvaT 
śarīrakaraṇākārāḥ puruṣārthaprasiddhaye 
bhogābhāvādvipadyante śarīrāṇi sahasradhā  SvaT 
pāśacchede vidhistasya mantraiśca vidhicoditaiḥ 
evaṃ pāśatrayasyāpi viśleṣo dīkṣayocyate  SvaT 
śarīraśeṣabhaṅgena ekacaitanyabhāvanā 
pūrṇāhutiṃ śivenaiva vauṣaḍjātiyutena ca  SvaT 
śuddhatattvāgrasaṃsthaṃ tac caitanyaṃ kanakaprabham 
uddhārāyāhutīstisraḥ punardhāmnā tu dāpayet  SvaT 
tasmāt tattvādgṛhītvā tu caitanyaṃ malasaṃyutam 
mudrayā prāgvidhānena ātmasthaṃ pūrayedddhṛdi  SvaT 
kumbhitvā recya saṃgṛhya dvādaśāntād dhruveṇa tu 
śiṣyadehe niveśyaitan nāḍīrandhreṇa pūrvavat  SvaT 
tatsthīkaraṇahetvarthaṃ dhāmnā caivāhutitrayam 
kalāśuddhyavasāne tu brahmāṇaṃ kāraṇādhipam  SvaT 
svanāmapraṇavāhvāna pūrvaṃ saṃtarpya cārpayet 
śabdasparśo tyajet tasmin dhruvādyau nāmasaṃyutau  SvaT 
svāhākāraprayogena tau brahmaṇi nivedayet 
tisṛbhistisṛbhirhomāt puryaṣṭāṃśaṃ nivedayet  SvaT 
āmantraṇavibhaktyā tu śrāvaṇāṃ tasya kārayet 
brahmāṇaṃ pūjayitvā tu homaṃ kṛtvā visarjayet  SvaT 
dhruveṇābhyarcya vāgīśīṃ saṃtarpya ca visarjayet 
hutvāvalokayettatra viśuddhaṃ pāśajālakam  SvaT 
prākkarmabhāvikasyātha abhāvaṃ bhāvayettadā 
mumukṣornirapekṣatvāt prārabdhrekaṃ na śodhayet  SvaT 
sādhakasya tu bhūtyarthaṃ prākkarmaikaṃ tu śodhayet 
prākkarmāgāmi caikasthaṃ bhāvayitvā ca dīkṣayet  SvaT 
śivadharmiṇyasau dīkṣā lokadharmiṇyato 'nyathā 
prāktanāgamikasyāpi adharmakṣayakāriṇī  SvaT 
lokadharmiṇyasau jñeyā mantrārādhanavarjitā 
prārabdhadehabhede tu bhuṅkte sa hyaṇimādikān  SvaT 
bhuktvā vrajedūrdhvaṃ guruṇā yatra yojitaḥ 
sakale niṣkale vāpi śiṣyācāryavaśādbhaved  SvaT 
nirvāṇe 'pi sabījāyāṃ karmābhāvādvipadyate 
samayācārapāśaṃ hi dīkṣitaḥ pālayettu yaḥ  SvaT 
taṃ pāśaṃ naiva śuddhyeta sā sabījā prakīrtitā 
samayācārapāśaṃ tu nirbījāyāṃ viśodhayet  SvaT 
dīkṣāmātreṇa muktiḥ syād bhakrimātrādguroḥ sadā 
sadyonirvāṇadā dīkṣā nirbījā sā dvitīyakā  SvaT 
atītanāgatārabdha pāśatrayaviyojikā 
dīkṣāvasāne śuddhiḥ syād dehatyāge paraṃ padam  SvaT 
evaṃ bhāvānusāreṇa śiṣyāṇāṃ guruṇā sadā 
phalaṃ tu vividhākāraṃ niṣpādyeta sudīkṣayā  SvaT 
acintyā mantraśaktirvai parameśamukhodbhavā 
kriyā kāle prayoktavyā guruṇā bhaktipūrvikā  SvaT 
viṣāṇamiva pāśānāṃ mantraiḥ kavalanaṃ dhruvam 
karoti mantratattvajñaḥ śivāveśī guruḥ kṣaṇāt  SvaT 
kalāsaṃdhānakaṃ kuryāc chuddhāśuddhadvirūpagam 
śuddhamuccārayedhrasvam aśuddhaṃ dīrghameva ca  SvaT 
ekatvaṃ bhāvayitvā tu līnaṃ śuddhaṃ vibhāvayet 
praṇavādinivṛttistu pratiṣṭhā tadanantaram  SvaT 
namaskārastadante tu kalāsaṃdhānakaṃ smṛtam 
āvāhya sthāpya saṃpūjyā hutīstisraḥ prapātayet  SvaT 
kalāsaṃdhānametaddhi vyāptiṃ tasyāvalokayet 
gulphādārabhya nābhyantaṃ śiṣyadehe 'dhvakalpanam  SvaT 
pratiṣṭhāyā bhavedvyāptiś caturviṃśatitattvikā 
ṣaṭpañcāśadbhuvanikā trayoviṃśativarṇikā  SvaT 
jñeyaikaviṃśatipadā trimantrā ca vidhīyate 
mukhyā hyete smṛtāḥ pāśāḥ sūkṣmānantarvibhāvayet  SvaT 
anyattantraprasiddhiṃ tu tanmātrendriyaśodhanam 
ṣaṭkośānviṣayān pañca tadantarbhāvayetsadā  SvaT 
viśeṣasthāpanaṃ kṛtvā pūjyā gandhādibhistataḥ 
bhairaveṇāhutīstisraḥ tasyā vāgīśikalpanā  SvaT 
svanāmāvāhanādyasya ardhahomādi pūrvavat 
prokṣaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ cheda ākarṣagrahaṇe tathā  SvaT 
dhāmnāpūrya kumbhayitvā chittvātha grāhayetpunaḥ 
yojanaṃ garbhadhāritvaṃ jananaṃ pūrvavatkramāt  SvaT 
aiśvarīṃ mūrtimāsthāya tāḍanādīni kārayet 
adhikārasthathā bhogo layo niṣkṛtireva ca  SvaT 
śivarūpeṇa kartavyāḥ niṣkṛtiḥ śirasā punaḥ 
viśleṣaśca hṛdā homyaḥ pāśacchedastathāsinā  SvaT 
pūrṇāhutisamuddhāraṃ pūrvavadbhairaveṇa tu 
sadāśivatanau sthitvā viśleṣādīni kārayet  SvaT 
ātmasthaṃ pūrakeṇaiva tatsthaṃ recakavṛttitaḥ 
svanāmnoccārayedviṣṇuṃ dhyātvāvāhya tu sthāpayet  SvaT 
pūjayetpuṣpagandhādyaiḥ tarpaṇāhutitrayam 
rasaṃ puryaṣṭakāṃśaṃ tu arpayedviṣṇave sadā  SvaT 
visarjayettato viṣṇuṃ vāgīśīṃ ca visarjayet 
kalāsaṃdhiryathāpūrvaṃ hrasvadīrghaprayogataḥ  SvaT 
abhāvaṃ bhāvayettasmin pāśajāle tvanantake 
kalādvayavinirmuktaḥ paśurūrdhvagamotsukaḥ  SvaT 
tasyedānīṃ tṛtīyasyāṃ vidyāyāṃ yojya śodhayet 
sthāpayitvā saṃpūjya juhuyādāhutitrayam  SvaT 
evaṃ tu saṃmukhīkṛtya prāgivādhvāvalokanam 
puṃstattvādyāvanmāyāntaṃ vidyāyā vyāptiriṣyate  SvaT 
sapta tattvāni bhuvana saptaviṃśatireva ca 
padaviṃśatirākhyātā varṇāḥ sapta prakīrtitāḥ  SvaT 
mantrau dvau ṣaḍvidhādhvānaṃ jñātvā vāgīśikalpanam 
praṇavena samāvāhya vyāpinīṃ sarvayoniṣu  SvaT 
samakālamṛtutvena dhyātvā saṃpūjya tarpayet 
tataḥ śivāmbhasā śiṣyaṃ prokṣya cāstreṇa tāḍayet  SvaT 
tenaiva cāstrabhūtena huṃphaṭkārayutena tu 
ātmano revakenaiva śiṣyadehe viśeddhṛdi  SvaT 
astramantreṇa saṃchedya viśeṣāśleṣyāstreṇa karṣayet 
dvādaśāntāttu saṃgṛhya ātmasthaṃ pūrvavatkuru  SvaT 
pūrakeṇātha saṃkumbhya recayitvā tu yojayet 
pūrvavaddvyāpakaṃ tasya caitanyaṃ sarvayoniṣu  SvaT 
yogādyaṃ layaparyantaṃ dhāmnā caivātra pūrvavat 
śikhayā śatahomāttu vidyāyā niṣkṛtirbhavet  SvaT 
praṇavādi tato rudram āvāhya sthāpya pūjayet 
tato 'sya vinyaseddevi gandharūpe dhruvāhutī  SvaT 
puryaṣakāṃśaṃ vinyasya visarjya rudradevatām 
vāgīśīṃ ca visarjyaivaṃ kalāsaṃdhiśca pūrvavat  SvaT 
hrasvadīrghavibhāgena vidyāṃ śāntau niyojayet 
saṃdhānārthaṃ tu mūlena juhuyādāhutitrayam  SvaT 
svanāmnāvāhanaṃ śānter vidhipūrvaṃ nivedanam 
prameyabhāvanāṃ kṛtvā pūjayet kusumādibhiḥ  SvaT 
trirāhutiṃ tu mūlena vidyātattvātsadāśivam 
tattvānāṃ tritaye vyāptir varṇānāṃ traya eva ca  SvaT 
padaikādaśikā jñeyā purāṇi daśa sapta ca 
mantrau dvau ṣaḍvidho 'dhvaivaṃ mukhyāḥ pāśā ime smṛtāḥ  SvaT 
sūkṣmapāśānanekāṃśca tadantarbhāvayetsadā 
vagīśīṃ kalpayettatra pūrveṇa vidhināhutiḥ  SvaT 
pūjanaṃ mūlamantreṇa tataḥ prokṣaṇatāḍanam 
chedākarṣagrahaṃ caiva yogadhāritvajanma ca  SvaT 
adhikārastathā bhogo layo vai pūrvavadbhavet 
sarve te mūlamantreṇa āhutitritayena tu  SvaT 
niṣkṛtau śatahomaṃ tu kavacena tu kārayet 
viśleṣaṃ pāśachedaṃ tu kuryādastreṇa daiśikaḥ  SvaT 
uddhārakaraṇātmastha tatsthīkārānbhavena tu 
svanāmnā praṇavādyena īśamāvāhya pūjayet  SvaT 
saṃpūjya hutvā saṃtarpya buddhyahaṃkṛtidyaṃśakam 
svanāmnā praṇavādyaṃ tu svāhānte buddhimarpayet  SvaT 
ahaṃkāraṃ tathāpyevaṃ hutvedaṃ kṣamayettataḥ 
vāgīśīṃ pūjayitvā tu tarpayitvā visarjayet  SvaT 
kalāsaṃdhānakaṃ pūrvaṃ śāntyatīte tu yojayet 
hrasvadīrghavibhāgena juhuyādāhutitrayam  SvaT 
dhruveṇa tattvasaṃdhānaṃ kartavyaṃ vidhivedinā 
kalopasthāpanaṃ paścād dhruveṇa juhuyātpriye  SvaT 
trirāhutiprayogeṇa svanāmapadamuccaran 
śāntyatītāṃ samāvāhya sthāpayetpūjayetpunaḥ  SvaT 
vyāptimālokya cādhvasthāṃ śivatattvagatāśca ye 
bindurnādastathā śaktiḥ śivatattve vyavasthitāḥ  SvaT 
padamekaṃ mantra eko varṇāḥ ṣoḍaśa kīrtitāḥ 
bhuvanāni tu sūkṣmāṇi śāntyatīte tu bhāvayet  SvaT 
śodhanīyā varārohe yāvatte śivaraśmayaḥ 
śivasyordhve śivo jñeyo yatra yukto na jāyate  SvaT 
ṣaḍadhvā caikato jñeyaḥ tasya saṃkhyāṃ punaḥ śṛṇu 
kalāśca pañca vijñeyās tattvaṣaṭtriśadeva tu  SvaT 
sacaturviṃśati jñeyaṃ bhuvanānāṃ śatadvayam 
ekāśītipadānyatra varṇārdhaśatikā smṛtā  SvaT 
mantrā ekādaśā jñeyā ityetaccādhvamaṇḍalam 
etasmiñśuddhimāpane muktimāpnoti dīkṣitaḥ  SvaT 
dhruveṇāvāhya vāgīśīṃ vinyaset pūrvavaddhutiḥ 
saṃpūjya kusumādayistu tadyonau pūrvavatpaśum  SvaT 
dhruveṇa sarvaṃ kartavyaṃ jananādilayāntakam 
niṣkṛtau śatahomaṃ tu mūlamantreṇa kalpayet  SvaT 
viśleṣapāśacchedābhyāṃ prāgvatkuryāddhruveṇa tu 
graheṇātmasthatatsthatvaṃ praṇavena paśoḥ smṛtam  SvaT 
sadāśivamathāvāhya mūlamantraṃ samuccaran 
namaskāreṇa saṃsthāpya puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjya tarpayet  SvaT 
manaḥ puryaṣṭakāṃśaṃ tu vinyasetkāraṇeśvare 
praṇavādi samuccārya manaḥsaṃjñāṃ namastathā  SvaT 
vinyasya pūjayetpaścāt saṃjñāsvāhāntameva ca 
āhutitritayaṃ hutvā puryaṣṭāṃśādviśuddhyati  SvaT 
tato visarjayeddevaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca sadāśivam 
puṣpādibhiḥ samabhyarcya vāgīśīṃ tadanantaram  SvaT 
tā tu saṃpūjya saṃtarpya vijñāpyā bhaktibhāvitā 
kṣamasva devadeveśi paśvarthaṃ kheditā mayā  SvaT 
idānīṃ noparoddhavyaṃ gaccha devi svaviṣṭapam 
visarjyaivaṃ kalā bhāvyā śāntyatītā layaṃ gatā  SvaT 
svaśaktyādhāraparyante susūkṣmābhāvasaṃsthite 
ātmatattvavibhāgena dhāmnā vai juhuyācchatam  SvaT 
saśaboccārayogena ātmatattve tu homayet 
māyātattvāvadhi jñeyaṃ daiśikena mahādhvare  SvaT 
vidhivaikalyakarmārthaṃ prāyaścittaviśuddhaye 
vidyātatve tu hotavyaṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ priye  SvaT 
upāṃśūccarayogena vidyātattve tu homayet 
sadāśivāntamadhvānaṃ vidyātattvaṃ vinirdiśet  SvaT 
mantroccaravolomena prāyaścittaṃ tu yadbhavet 
tadviśuddhyai sa homaḥ syād vidyātattve tu yaḥ kṛtaḥ  SvaT 
manovijñānavaikalyāt prāyaścittaṃ tu yadbhavet 
tacchuddhyarthaṃ śive tattve mūlamantreṇa homayet  SvaT 
mānasena prayogena śaktyante 'dhvani saṃsthitam 
tattvatrayaviśuddhyante śikhācchedaṃ tu kalpayet  SvaT 
adhvāntasthāṃ parāṃ śāntām anaupamyāmanāmayām 
vyāpinīṃ sarvatattvānāṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam  SvaT 
dhyātvā śiśoḥ śikhāgre tu puṣpāgre jalabinduvat 
kartarīṃ śikhayāmantrya śikhayā cchedayecchikhām  SvaT 
śikhāṃ samarpya cānyasya nirgacchetsa saśiṣyakaḥ 
snānaṃ samācarecchiṣyaḥ gurorācamanaṃ bhavet  SvaT 
snānamuddhūlanaṃ vātha ācaretsvecchayā guruḥ 
praviśya sakalīkṛtya pūrṇayā juhuyācchikhām  SvaT 
hutvā nirgamya cācamyā kṣālya sruksruvakartarīḥ 
praviśya sakalīkṛtya śivahastānupūjanam  SvaT 
tatastu maṇḍale paścāt pūjayetparameśvaram 
puṣpādibhiraśeṣaistu tato vijñāpayecchivam  SvaT 
bhagavaṃstvatprasādena adhvaṣṭakavyavasthitam 
paśuṃ saṃgṛhya saṃśodhya śikhācchedāvasānakam  SvaT 
tvanmukhoktavidhānaṃ tu leśato vartitaṃ mayā 
tvacchaktyaiva tu gantavyam āśu dhruvapadaṃ śivam  SvaT 
idānīṃ yojane karma tavājñānuvidhāyinaḥ 
ājñā me dīyatāṃ nātha śiṣyaṃ saṃyojayāmyaham  SvaT 
labdhānujñātamātmānaṃ prahṛṣṭo nirgataḥ purāt 
ardhahasto vrajedagnim śiṣyamāhūya prokṣayet  SvaT 
pūrvavaccāsanasthasya sakalīkaraṇādikam 
antaḥkaraṇavinyāsaṃ nāḍīsaṃdhānapūrvakam  SvaT 
pūjanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ cāgnau mantrāṇāṃ ca śivasya ca 
daśabhāgavibhāgena yathā dravyānusārataḥ  SvaT 
mantrānsaṃśodhayetpaścāt sakalīkaraṇe sthitān 
sakṛdāhutiyogena adhikāro vivarjyatām  SvaT 
sakalīkaraṇatvena na kadācitpaśoḥ punaḥ 
yojanīyaṃ prayogaṃ tu adhunā kathayāmi te  SvaT 
jñātvā cārapramāṇaṃ tu prāṇasaṃcārameva ca 
ṣaḍvidhādhvavibhāgaṃ tu prāṇaikatra yathāsthitam  SvaT 
haṃsoccāraṃ tu varṇaiśca kāraṇatyāgameva ca 
śūnyaṃ samarasaṃ jñeyaṃ tyāgaṃ saṃyogamudbhavam  SvaT 
bhedanaṃ ca padārthānāṃ bhāvaprāptivaśātpunaḥ 
ātmavidyāśivavyāptim evaṃ jñātvā tu yojayet  SvaT 
tadvibhāgaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathā jñāyeta tattvataḥ 
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulaścāro hṛtpadmādyāvaśaktitaḥ  SvaT 
tuṭiṣoḍaśamānena kālena kalitaḥ priye 
saṃcarantaṃ vibhāgena yathāvattaṃ śṛṇuṣva me  SvaT 
hṛtpadmādyāvadayanaṃ bhāgamekaṃ tyajettu saḥ 
nāsikāgre dvitīyaṃ tu śaktyante tu tṛtīyakam  SvaT 
tatrastho vinivarteta yāvattattvaṃ na vindati 
vidite tu pare tattve tatrastho 'pi na bādhyate  SvaT 
śaktyā cādho yadā gacched abudhastu tadā bhavet 
hṛdgataḥ punaruttiṣṭhed budhyamānaḥ sa ucyate  SvaT 
śaktiṃ prāpya budho jñeyaḥ vyāpinyaṃśe prabuddhatā 
atītaḥ suprabuddhastu unmanastvaṃ tadā bhavet  SvaT 
na kālo na kalā cāro na tattvaṃ naca kāraṇam 
sunirvāṇaṃ paraṃ śuddhaṃ gurupāramparāgatam  SvaT 
tadvoditvā vimucyeta gatvā bhūyo na jāyate 
adhvaṣṭkaṃ yathā prāṇe saṃsthitaṃ kathayāmi te  SvaT 
āpādānmūrdhaparyantaṃ citeḥ saṃvedanaṃ hi yat 
bhuvanādhvā sa vijñeyas tattvādhvā ca tathaiva hi  SvaT 
kalākalitasaṃtānaḥ prāṇaḥ saṃcarate sadā 
nivṛttiśca pratiṣṭhā ca adhobhāge pravartike  SvaT 
vidyā śāntistathā cordhve śāntyatītā tvadhiṣṭhikā 
tadatītaḥ paro bhāvaḥ tadūrdhvam padamavyayam  SvaT 
evaṃ bindukalā jñeyā nādaśaktyātmikāśca yāḥ 
vyāpinyādyātmikā yāśca vyāpyavyāpakabhedataḥ  SvaT 
prāṇaikasaṃsthitāḥ sarvāḥ ṣaṭtyāgātsaptame layaḥ 
kalādhvaivaṃ samākhyāto varṇādhvānaṃ nibodha me  SvaT 
varṇāḥ śabdātmakāḥ sarve jagatyasmiṃścarācare 
sthitāḥ pañcaśatā bhedaiḥ śāstreṣvānantyakoṭiṣu  SvaT 
śabdātprāṇaḥ samākhyātas tasmādvarṇāstu prāṇataḥ 
utpadyante layaṃ yānti yatra śabdo layaṃ gataḥ  SvaT 
śabdātīto varārohe tattvena saha yujyate 
yuktaḥ sarvagato devi dharmādharmavivarjitaḥ  SvaT 
nādho nirīkṣate bhūyaḥ śivatattvaṃ gato yadā 
adho vai yātyadharmeṇa dharmeṇordhvaṃ vrajetpunaḥ  SvaT 
vijñānena dvayaṃ tyaktvā sarvagastu bhavediha 
varṇādhvaivaṃ samākhyātaḥ padādhvā procyate 'dhunā  SvaT 
ekāśītipadānyeva vidyārājasthitānyapi 
varṇātmakāni tānyatra varṇāḥ prāṇātmakāḥ sthitāḥ  SvaT 
tasmādevaṃ padānyatra tāni prāṇakrameṇa tu 
padādhvaivaṃ samākhyātaḥ mantrādhvānaṃ nibodha me  SvaT 
mantrikādaśikā yā tu sā ca haṃse vyavasthitā 
padikādaśikā sā ca prāṇe carati nityaśaḥ  SvaT 
akāraśca ukāraśca makāro bindureva ca 
ardhacandro nirodhī ca nādo nādānta eva ca  SvaT 
śaktiśca vyāpinī caiva samanaikādaśī smṛtā 
unmanā ca tato 'tītā tadatītaṃ nirāmayam  SvaT 
mantrā evaṃ sthitāḥ prāṇe haṃsoccārastathocyate 
hakārastu smṛtaḥ prāṇaḥ svapravṛtto halākṛtiḥ  SvaT 
akāreṇa yadā yukta ukāracaraṇena tu 
makāramātrayā yukto varṇoccāro bhavetsphuṭaḥ  SvaT 
binduḥ śiraḥsamāyogāt susvaratvaṃ prapadyate 
nādo 'sya vadanaṃ proktaḥ vadanaṃ śabdamīrayet  SvaT 
anenaiva ca yogena haṃsaḥ puruṣa ucyate 
brahmaviṣṇvīśamārgeṇa caranvai sarvajantuṣu  SvaT 
śaktitattve layaṃ yāti vijñānenordhvatāṃ vrajet 
vyāpinīṃ samanāṃ tyaktvā vrajedunmanayā śivam  SvaT 
śivatattvagato haṃso na caret vyāpako bhavet 
haṃsoccāraḥ samākhyātaḥ kāraṇaiśca samanvitaḥ  SvaT 
hakāraḥ prāṇaśaktyātmā akāro brahmavācakaḥ 
hṛdi tyāgo bhavettasya ukāro viṣṇuvācakaḥ  SvaT 
kaṇṭhe tyāgo bhavettasya makāro rudravācakaḥ 
tālumadhye tyajettaṃ tu binduścaiveśvaraḥ svayam  SvaT 
tyāgastatra bhruvormadhye nāde vācyaḥ sadāśivaḥ 
lalāṭānmūrdhaparyantaṃ tyāgastasya vidhīyate  SvaT 
śaktivyāpinīsamanās tāsāṃ vācyaḥ śivo 'vyayaḥ 
mūrdhamadhye tyajecchaktiṃ tadūrdhve vyāpinīṃ tyajet  SvaT 
samanāṃ unmanāṃ tyaktvā ṣaṭtyāgātsaptame layaḥ 
sūkṣmasūkṣmatarairbhāvair evamevaṃ tyajetpriye  SvaT 
sthūlasthūlatarairbhāvair nānāsiddhiphalapradaiḥ 
sūkṣmo 'tyantaṃ paro bhāvas tv abhāvaḥ sa vidhīyate  SvaT 
unmanā tvaparo bhāvaḥ sthūlastasyāparo mataḥ 
tasyāparaṃ punaḥ śūnyaṃ saṃsparśaṃ ca tato 'param  SvaT 
śabdo jyotiḥ tato mantrāḥ kāraṇā bhuvanāni ca 
pañcabhūtātmabhuvanaṃ kāraṇaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitam  SvaT 
bhuvanaṃ cintayedyastu vakṣyamāṇaikarūpakam 
bhuvaneśatvamāpnoti śivaṃ dhyātvā tu tanmayaḥ  SvaT 
brahmādikāraṇānāṃ ca sādhane vigrahaṃ smaran 
pūrvoktalakṣaṇaṃ yaśca tanmayatvamavāpnuyāt  SvaT 
mantriśca mantrasiddhistu japahomārcanādbhavet 
pūrvoktarūpakadhyānāt siddhyantyatra na saṃśayaḥ  SvaT 
jyotirdhyānāttu yogīndro yogasiddhimavāpnuyāt 
tanmayatvaṃ yadāpnoti yogināmadhipo bhavet  SvaT 
śabdadhyānācca śabdātmā vāṅmayāpūrako bhavet 
sparśadhyānācca sparśātmā jagataḥ kāraṇaṃ bhavet  SvaT 
śūnyadhyānācca śūnyātmā vyāpī sarvagato bhavet 
samanadhyānayogena yogī sarvajñatāṃ vrajet  SvaT 
unmanyā tu paraṃ sūkṣmam abhāvaṃ bhāvayetsadā 
sarvendriyamanotītas tv alakṣyo 'bhāva ucyate  SvaT 
abhāvaṃ bhāvyaṃ bhāvena bhāvaṃ kṛtvā nirāśrayam 
sarvopādhivinirmuktam abhāvaṃ labhate padam  SvaT 
eṣa te kāraṇatyāgaḥ kālatyāgaṃ nibodha me 
tuṭiṣoḍaśasaṃyuktaḥ prāṇastu samudāhṛtaḥ  SvaT 
tuṭadvayaṃ samāśritya ekaiko bhairavaḥ sthitaḥ 
ahorātravibhāgena kurvantyudayameva te  SvaT 
navamastu paro devaḥ tejasastūdayanti te 
sarvaṃ kālaṃ tyajetprāṇe yathāvatkathayāmi te  SvaT 
tuṭayaḥ ṣoḍaśaivoktāḥ kālasya karaṇaṃ tu tāḥ 
tadādiḥ saṃsthitaḥ kālaḥ sarvaṃ carati vāṅmayam  SvaT 
tuṭirlavo nimeṣaśca kāṣṭhā caiva kalā tathā 
muhūrtaścāpyahorātraḥ pakṣo māsa ṛtustathā  SvaT 
ayanaṃ vatsaraścaiva yugaṃ manvantaraṃ tathā 
kalpaścaiva mahākalpaḥ śaktyante taṃ parityajet  SvaT 
vyāpinyante paraḥ kālaḥ sa tadaṅgī tyajettu tam 
sa ca saptadaśo jñeyaḥ parārdhaparataḥ sthitaḥ  SvaT 
 parārdhaḥ corr
so 'pi cāṣṭādaśo devi samanānte tu taṃ tyajet 
sarvakālaṃ tu kālasya vyāpakaḥ paramo 'vyayaḥ  SvaT 
unmanyante pare yojyo na kālastatra vidyate 
nityo nityodito vyāpī ādirūpaṃ na saṃtyajet  SvaT 
taṃ ca nityoditaṃ prāpya tanmayo jāyate sadā 
kālatyāgo bhavedevaṃ śūnyabhāvastvathocyate  SvaT 
ūrdhvaśūnyamadhaḥśūnyaṃ madhyaśūnyaṃ tṛtīyakam 
śūnyatrayaṃ calaṃ hyetat tadadho madhya ūrdhvataḥ  SvaT 
caturthaṃ vyāpinīśūnyaṃ samanāyāṃ ca pañcamam 
unmanāyāṃ tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ ṣaḍete sāmayāḥ sthitāḥ  SvaT 
tattvenādhiṣṭhitāḥ sarve sāmayā api siddhidāḥ 
ṣaṭ śūnyāni parityajya saptame tu layaṃ kuru  SvaT 
tacchūnyaṃ tu paraṃ sūkṣmaṃ sarvāvasthāvivarjitam 
aśūnyaṃ śūnyamityuktaṃ śūnyaṃ cābhāva ucyate  SvaT 
abhāvaḥ sa samuddiṣṭo yatra bhāvāḥ kṣayaṃ gatāḥ 
sattāmātraṃ paraṃ śāntaṃ tatpadaṃ kimapi sthitam  SvaT 
yatra yatra ca nādādi sthūlā anye 'pi saṃsthitāḥ 
tatra tatra paraṃ śūnyaṃ sarvaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitam  SvaT 
tadeva bhavati sthūlaṃ sthūlopādhivaśātpriye 
sthūlasūkṣmaprabhedena tadekaṃ saṃvyavasthitam  SvaT 
tatprāpya tanmayatvaṃ ca labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ 
śūnyabhāvaḥ samākhyātaḥ sāmarasyaṃ nibodha me  SvaT 
ātmanyekaḥ samaraso mantre jñeyo dvitīyakaḥ 
tṛtīyaṃ nāḍigaṃ kuryāc chaktau kuryāccaturthakam  SvaT 
vyāpinyāṃ pañcamaṃ proktaṃ samanāyāṃ tu ṣaṣṭhakam 
tātvaḥ samaraso devi saptamastu vidhīyate  SvaT 
śiṣyātmānaṃ tu saṃgṛhya pūrvoktavidhinā kramāt 
paścādātmani saṃyojya lolībhūtaṃ vicintayet  SvaT 
pūrakaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā samānena nirodhayet 
yāvatyo nāḍayo devi tiryagūrdhvamadhaḥsthitāḥ  SvaT 
samānena samākṛṣṭā ekībhūtā bhavanti tāḥ 
tāsu ye vāyavaste 'pi prāṇe samarasīgatāḥ  SvaT 
nāḍayastu suṣumnāyām ekībhūtā vyavasthitāḥ 
tato vai uccarenmantraḥ nāde līnaṃ vicintayet  SvaT 
mantra ātmā tathā nāḍī evaṃ samarasībhavet 
vāmadakṣiṇamadhye tu tato nādaṃ pramocayet  SvaT 
setubandhaṃ ca taṃ mārgaṃ yatra gatvā na jāyate 
brahmā viṣṇuśca rudraśca īśvaraḥ śiva eva ca  SvaT 
ete 'tra samatāṃ yānti anyathā tu pṛthak pṛthak 
tasminsamuccarennādaṃ yāvacchaktau layaṃ gataḥ  SvaT 
śaktimadhyagato nādaḥ śaktyātmā tu vidhīyate 
sarvaṃ śaktimayaṃ tatra sarvaṃ samarasībhavet  SvaT 
tadūrdhvaṃ vyāpinīṃ prāpya sarvaṃ tanmayatāṃ vrajet 
samantādvyāpnuyādyasmād vyāpinītyabhidhīyate  SvaT 
tadūrdhvaṃ samanāṃ vyāpya tanmayatvaṃ vrajetpunaḥ 
sā ca sarvagatā jñeyā sāmarasyena saṃsthitā  SvaT 
ṣaṣṭhaṃ samarasaṃ tyaktvā saptamaṃ tu tato vrajet 
taṃ prāpya tanmayatvaṃ hi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā  SvaT 
sa ca sarveṣu bhūteṣu bhāvatatvendriyeṣu ca 
sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva cetanācetanasthitam  SvaT 
adhvānaṃ vyāpya sarvaṃ tu sāmarasyena saṃsthitaḥ 
prasahya cañcalītyeva yogināmapi yanmanaḥ  SvaT 
yasya jñeyamayo bhāvaḥ sthiraḥ pūrṇaḥ samantataḥ 
mano na calate tasya sarvāvasthāgatasya tu  SvaT 
yatra yatra mano yāti jñeyaṃ tatraiva cintayet 
calitvā yāsyate kutra sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ yataḥ  SvaT 
viṣayeṣu ca sarveṣu indriyārtheṣu ca sthitaḥ 
yatra yatra nirūpyeta nāśivaṃ vidyate kvacit  SvaT 
evāṃ samarasaṃ jñātvā nāsau muhyet kadācana 
yasyaivaṃ sarvato bhāvaḥ so 'pi sarvagato bhavet  SvaT 
evaṃ samarasaḥ prokto viṣuvattu nibodha me 
prathamaṃ prāṇaviṣuvan mātraṃ jñeyaṃ dvitīyakam  SvaT 
tṛtīyaṃ nāḍiviṣuvat praśāntaṃ ca caturthakam 
pañcamaṃ śaktiviṣuvat ṣaṣṭhaṃ vai kāla ucyate  SvaT 
saptama tattvaviṣuvat pravibhāgastvathocyate 
ātmānaṃ ca manaḥ prāṇe saṃyojya viṣuvadbhavet  SvaT 
prāṇe viṣuvadākhyātaṃ māntraṃ viṣuvaducyate 
mantramuccārayettāvad yāvannānyamanā bhavet  SvaT 
parāparavibhāgena mantrātmā tu taducyate 
māntraṃ viṣuvadityuktaṃ nāḍisthaṃ tannibodha me  SvaT 
sarvāsāmeva nāḍīnāṃ madhye yā saṃvyavasthitā 
suṣumnā nāma sā jñeyā nābheḥ śaktyā śivaṃ gatā  SvaT 
tatra pravāhayennādaṃ nāḍīviṣuvaducyate 
praśāntaṃ viṣuvaccaivam adhunā kathayāmi te  SvaT 
ayane ṣaḍaṅgulaścāraḥ kāraṇānyaṅgule 'ṅgule 
tānyadhastātparityajya kāraṇāni ṣaḍeva tu  SvaT 
saptame tu praśāntaṃ vai praśāntendriyagocaram 
praśāntaḥ stimito jñeyaḥ stimito niścalaḥ smṛtaḥ  SvaT 
niścalo nistaraṅgaśca sthiraḥ pūrṇaḥ samantataḥ 
evaṃbhāvaṃ samāsthāya dīkṣā kāryā tu daiśikaiḥ  SvaT 
etatpraśāntaviṣuvat śaktyupādhiṃ nibodha me 
śaktimadhyagato nādo nādordhvaṃ ca caredyadā  SvaT 
tāvattu śaktiviṣuvat kālākhyaṃ tu nibodha me 
tuṭiḥ ṣoḍaśakā yā tu prāṇānte saṃvyavasthitā  SvaT 
kālo bhrūkṣepamātrastu tatrānte kīrtito mayā 
taṃ parāparabhāgena punareva tridhā kuru  SvaT 
aparaḥ ṣoḍaśo yāvat kālaḥ saptadaśaḥ paraḥ 
parāparastu yaḥ kālaḥ sa priye 'ṣṭādaśaḥ prabhuḥ  SvaT 
prāṇa evaṃ tridhā kālaṃ kṛtvā caiva tyajetpunaḥ 
aparaḥ śaktimūrdhastho vyāpinyāṃ ca dvitīyakaḥ  SvaT 
tṛtīyaḥ samanāsthāne tatkālaviṣuvatsmṛtam 
etatṣaṣṭhaṃ samākhyātaṃ saptamaṃ tātvvamucyate  SvaT 
unmanā parato devi tatrātmānaṃ niyojayet 
tasminyuktastato hyātmā tanmayaśca prajāyate  SvaT 
tattvākhyaṃ viṣuvaddevi sarveṣāṃ parataḥ sthitam 
viṣuvadevaṃvidhaṃ jñātvā ko na mucyeta bandhanāt  SvaT 
viṣuvatte samākhyātaṃ padārthabhedanaṃ śṛṇu 
tyāgaṃ cānubhavaṃ caiva yojanaṃ ca pare pade  SvaT 
padārthaikādaśī jñeyā unmanāntaḥ paro bhavet 
bhedayejjñānaśūlena jñānaṃ jñeyasya jñāpakam  SvaT 
jñāpakaṃ bodhamatulaṃ dīpavadyotanaṃ yataḥ 
dīpahasto yathā kaścid dravyamālokya cāharet  SvaT 
evaṃ jñānena ca jñeyaṃ tasmin kuryāttu saṃsthitam 
jñānaṃ vai lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ jñeyatatvasya suvrate  SvaT 
lakṣaṇaṃ guṇa ākhyātaḥ kalā tattvasya sarvadā 
na guṇena vinā tattvaṃ na tattvena vinā guṇaḥ  SvaT 
guṇaṃ gṛhṇanti sarvatra na tattvaṃ gṛhyate kvacit 
gṛhyate hyanumānena pratyakānubhavena ca  SvaT 
arthipratyarthibhāvena āgamena tu labhyate 
āgamo jñānamiyuktam anantāḥ śāstrakoṭayaḥ  SvaT 
śāstraṃ śabdātmakaṃ sarvaṃ śabdo haṃsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
haṃsayogaḥ purākhyātaḥ mātrāsaṃkhyā tvathocyate  SvaT 
mātrāyogo yathā cāsya pramāṇaṃ hṛdayādisu 
nābherūrdhvaṃ vitastyante kaṇṭhādhastātṣaḍaṅgule  SvaT 
hṛdayaṃ madhyadeśe tu caturaṅgulasaṃmitam 
caturviṃśatitattvaistu brahmā tatra vyavasthitaḥ  SvaT 
kaṇṭhamaṣṭāṅgulaṃ viddhi viṣṇustatra vyavasthitaḥ 
tattvāṣṭakena saṃyuktaḥ tadūrdhvaṃ caturaṅgulam  SvaT 
māyātattvaṃ samāśritya rudrastālutale sthitaḥ 
aṅguladvayamānaṃ tu bhruvormadhyaṃ prakīrtitam  SvaT 
tatreśvaraḥ sthito devi tattvadvayasamanvitaḥ 
ekādaśāṅgule caiva mūrdhvaṃ devaḥ sadāśivaḥ  SvaT 
tattvadvayasamāyukto yāvadbrahmabilaṃ gataḥ 
tadūrdhvaikāṅgulā śaktiḥ śivastatra vyavasthitaḥ  SvaT 
tvakcheṣe vyāpinī proktā samanā conmanā tataḥ 
tatparaṃ tu paraṃ tattvaṃ pramāṇaparivarjitam  SvaT 
mātrāsaṃkhyā ca yogaścā dhunā haṃsasya kathyate 
akāraśca hakāraśca dvāvetāvekataḥ sthitau  SvaT 
vibhaktirnānayorasti mārutāmbarayoriva 
ekamātraḥ sa vijñeyo hṛdayātsaṃpravartate  SvaT 
ukārastu dvimātro vai kaṇṭhasthāne samuccaret 
trimātrastu makāro vai tālumadhyagataścaret  SvaT 
binduścaivārdhamātrastu mātrārdhaṃ hi sa ucyate 
bhruvormadhye sa uccāras tasya devi vidhīyate  SvaT 
taccheṣāccārdhacandrastu pādamātrastvasau bhavet 
nirodhī cārdhapādastu lalāṭānte samuccaret  SvaT 
nādaḥ ṣoḍaśakāṃśastu mūrdhāntaṃ yāvaduccaret 
dvātriṃśadaṃśā śaktistu ṣaṭtriṃśānte samuccaret  SvaT 
vyāpinī catuḥṣaṣṭyaṃśā śaktestu parataḥsthitā 
samanā conmanā cordhvam amātraḥ paramo 'vyayaḥ  SvaT 
mātrāsaṃkhyā ca yogaśca pramāṇaṃ parikīrtitam 
evaṃ jñātvā varārohe padārthān bhedayettataḥ  SvaT 
bhedayenmatraśūlena mudrābhāvayutena ca 
mantro vai jñānaśaktiśca mudrā caiva kriyātmikā  SvaT 
bhāvaśca mana ityuktaṃ tanmano buddhipūrvakam 
paraśca manasā gamya icchāśaktyā tvadhiṣṭhitaḥ  SvaT 
yatra yatra bhavedicchā jñānaṃ tatra pravartate 
kriyākaraṇasaṃbandhāt tattvasyoccāraṇaṃ bhavet  SvaT 
kriyākaraṇahīnasya na caivoccāraṇaṃ bhavet 
kriyā karaṇabhedena sā caiva trividhā smṛtā  SvaT 
ekenoccārayettattvaṃ karaṇena vicakṣaṇaḥ 
nāḍīścātha dvitīyena dvārāṇi ca nirodhayet  SvaT 
tṛtīyaṃ karaṇaṃ divyaṃ kṛtvā vai tattvamuccaret 
pūrakaṃ kumbhakaṃ kṛtvā sarvadvārāṇi rodhayet  SvaT 
gudadvāreṇa ruddhena ruddhānyatra bhavanti hi 
dvāramekaṃ tataścordhve pravahattadvicintayet  SvaT 
nāḍayo granthipadmāśca ye 'dhomukhagatāḥ priye 
te kumbhakena saṃruddhā vikasanti samantataḥ  SvaT 
karaṇaṃ tu tataḥ kṛtvā lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vai śṛṇu 
jihvā tu tāluke yojyā kiṃcidūrdhvaṃ na saṃspṛśet  SvaT 
īṣatprasārya vaktraṃ tu kiṃcidoṣṭhau na saṃspṛśet 
dantapaṅktī tathaiveha dṛṣṭiścādhordhvavarjitā  SvaT 
kāyaṃ samunnataṃ kṛtvā karaṇaṃ divyamucyate 
divyaṃ ca karaṇaṃ kṛtvā tattvasyoccāraṇaṃ kuru  SvaT 
kumbhitaścaiva yaḥ prāṇo recayettaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ 
nāḍayo granthipadmāśca dehe yāḥsaṃvyavasthitāḥ  SvaT 
recakena samākṣiptā ūrdhvasroto bhavanti te 
tato vai jñānaśūlena granthīnbhindan samuccaret  SvaT 
bhitvā hṛtpadmagranthiṃ tu tataḥ śabdaḥ prajāyate 
yadākāśasamāyogāt ghoṣaśabdopamo bhavet  SvaT 
kaṇṭhastho viramecchabdaḥ kaṇṭhaṃ prāpya varānane 
bhindataḥ kaṇṭhadeśaṃ tu śabdo dhugadhugāyate  SvaT 
tālumadhyagataḥ prāṇo yadā bhavati suvrate 
bindatastālugranthiṃ tu śabdo ghumaghumāyate  SvaT 
evaṃ te 'nubhavāḥ proktāḥ prāṇe carati suvrate 
trayaste 'ṣṭakalāḥ proktā uparyuparitaḥ kramāt  SvaT 
tiṣṭhetsa yatra vai prāṇa ātmā tadgatimāpnuyāt 
tattadrūpaṃ bhavettasya sthānabhāvānurūpataḥ  SvaT 
bhruvormadhyaṃ yadā gacchet sphoṭaśabdastu jāyate 
binduṃ bhedayato devi śabdo dhumadhumāyate  SvaT 
kapirvai nārikīlena ācāryaḥ saha bindunā 
abhinnena kuto mokṣaṃ sabāhyābhyantaraṃ priye  SvaT 
bhitvā binduṃ tato devi ardhacandraṃ vibhedayet 
bhidyataścārdhacandrasya lalāṭe jhimijhimāyate  SvaT 
ardhacandraṃ tu bhittvā vai bhedayettu nirodhinīm 
tasyāstu bhidyamānāyāḥ śabdaḥ simisimāyate  SvaT 
sthanatrayamidaṃ devi pañcapañcakalānvitam 
prāṇasya caratastatra yasminsthāne sa tiṣṭhati  SvaT 
tattadrūpo bhavedātmā tāṃ tāṃ gatimavāpnuyāt 
nirodhinīṃ bhedayitvā tato nādaṃ vrajedbudhaḥ  SvaT 
vaṃśaśabdasamaḥ śabdas tatra sūkṣmaḥ prajāyate 
bhedayennādasaṃsthānaṃ brahmarandhraṃ sudurbhidam  SvaT 
bhidyato brahmarandhrasya śabdaḥ śumaśumāyate 
śaktimadhyagataḥ prāṇo vaṃśanādāntasaṃnibhaḥ  SvaT 
tāṃ vai tu bhedayecchaktiṃ durbhedyāṃ sarvayoginām 
bhidyate ca yadā śaktiḥ śāntaḥ śumaśumastataḥ  SvaT 
śaktiṃ bhitvā tato devi yaccheṣaṃ vyāpinī bhavet 
anubhāvo bavettatra sparśo yadvatpipīlikā  SvaT 
sthānatrayamidaṃ devi pañcapañcakalānvitam 
yatra yatra caretprāṇas tattadrūpamavāpnuyāt  SvaT 
yatra yatrāvatiṣṭheta tāṃ tāṃ gatimavāpnuyāt 
tasmādvai suprayatnena bhitvā yāti parāṃ gatim  SvaT 
bhitvā vai vyāpinīṃ devi samanāyāṃ manastyajet 
manasā tu manastyaktvā jīvaḥ kevalatāṃ vrajet  SvaT 
jīvo vai kevalastatra ātmajñānakriyānvitaḥ 
bandhanāśeṣanirmuktaḥ sattāmātrasvarūpakaḥ  SvaT 
samastādhvapadātītaḥ śuddhavijñānakevalaḥ 
gṛhāṇāti nāparaṃ bhāvaṃ na paraṃ ca śivātmakam  SvaT 
parāparavinirmuktaḥ svātmanyātmā vyavasthitaḥ 
ātmavyāptirbhavedeṣā śivavyāptirataḥ param  SvaT 
bandhanāśeṣabhāvena sarvādhvopādhivarjitā 
aviditvā paraṃ tattvaṃ śivatvaṃ kalpitaṃ tu yaiḥ  SvaT 
ta ātmopāsakāḥ śaive na gacchanti paraṃ śivam 
ātmatattvagatiṃ yānti ātmatattvānurañjitāḥ  SvaT 
tasmādātmā parityājyo yadīcchecchivamātmanaḥ 
ātmatattvaṃ tatastyājyaṃ vidyātatve niyojayet  SvaT 
unmanā sā tu vijñeyā manaḥ saṃkalpa ucyate 
saṃkalpaḥ kramato jñānam unmānaṃ yugapatsthitam  SvaT 
tasmāt sā tu parā vidyā yasmādanyā na vidyate 
vindate hyatra yugapat sārvajñyādiguṇān parān  SvaT 
vedanānādidharmasya paramātmatvabodhanā 
varjanā paramātmatve tasmādvidyeti socyate  SvaT 
tatrastho vyañjayettejaḥ paraṃ paramakāraṇam 
parasmiṃstejasi vyakte tatrasthaḥ śivatāṃ vrajet  SvaT 
supradīpte yathā vahnau śikhā dṛśyeta cāmbare 
dehaprāṇasthito hyātmā tadvallīyeta tatpade  SvaT 
tadvadevābhimānastu kartavyo daiśikottamaiḥ 
ahameva paro haṃsaḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam  SvaT 
matprāṇe sa tu paśvātmā līnaḥ samarasīgataḥ 
mantrakaraṇakriyāyogād yojayāmi pare śive  SvaT 
evaṃ yo vetti tattvena agnivaddehamadhyataḥ 
yadvadvahniśikhātītā tadvadyojayate pare  SvaT 
tasminyuktaḥ pare tattve sārvajñyādiguṇānvitaḥ 
śiva eko bhaveddevi avibhāgena sarvataḥ  SvaT 
tattvatrayaṃ paraṃ khyātam aparaṃ cādhvamadhyagam 
bhedanaṃ tu padārthānāṃ tyāgānubhavayojanam  SvaT 
pūrvoktaṃ ca idaṃ sarvaṃ jñātvā tattve niyojayet 
saṃkṣepeṇa tu tattvasya vyāptiṃ śṛṇu sureśvari  SvaT 
vidyātattvāspadaṃ baddhvā bindutattvāsane sthitaḥ 
nādaśaktitanuścaiva vyāpinīkaraṇānvitaḥ  SvaT 
sarvajñatvāvabodhena samanāntaścarā tu sā 
tritatvaṃ yatparaṃ proktaṃ tena cāpūritā tanuḥ  SvaT 
aparā sā tanuḥ sthūlā ṣaṭviṃśattattvakalpitā 
tattvatrayaṃ paraṃ yacca sarvatattvādhvavarjitam  SvaT 
tena cāpūritāśeṣaṃ sā tattvādhvaparā tanuḥ 
evamācarate yastu ācāraṃ tu śivātmakam  SvaT 
śivena sahacāritvād ācāryastena cocyate 
tasya darśanasaṃbhāṣā sparśanātsmaraṇādapi  SvaT 
bhavatyevaiśvarī vyāptir na bhavettadadhogatiḥ 
tena saṃyojito jantuḥ brahmahāpi śivo bhavet  SvaT 
tatastena samo nāsti jagatyasmiṃścarācare 
śiva ācāryarūpeṇa lokānugrahakārakaḥ  SvaT 
tasmānna mānavīṃ buddhiṃ kārayeddeśakaṃ prati 
ācāryasya ca mantrasya śivajñāne śivasya ca  SvaT 
nānātvaṃ naiva kurvanti vidyeśāścakranāyakāḥ 
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā vai vīravandite  SvaT 
ācāryatve niyuktā ye te sarve tu śivāḥ smṛtāḥ 
anyathā prāksvarūpeṇa ye paśyanti narādhamāḥ  SvaT 
narake te prapacyante sādākhyaṃ vatsaratrayam 
na tena saha saṃbhāṣā kartavyā tu śivārthinā  SvaT 
kṛtvā saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ tena narakaṃ so 'pi gacchati 
tasmācchivasamāḥ sarve draṣṭavyā muktimicchatā  SvaT 
bhuktimuktiphalāvāptir bhavatyeva tadājñayā 
ācāryaḥ svajānānāṃ ca kulakoṭisahasraśaḥ  SvaT 
jñānajñeyaparijñānāt samastāstārayiṣyati 
evamuktavidhānajño bhāvajñaścāpi daiśikaḥ  SvaT 
pūrṇāhutyaikayaivāsau paśūnyojayate pare 
pūrṇāhutiprayogaṃ tu kathayāmyadhunā tava  SvaT 
ūrdhvakāya ṛjugrīvaḥ samapādo vyavasthitaḥ 
nābhisthāne sruco mūlam uttānāgramukhaṃ samam  SvaT 
srucyupari sruvaṃ devi kṛtvā caivamadhomukham 
puṣpaṃ dattvā srugagre tu darbheṇa sahitau karau  SvaT 
muṣṭinā caiva hastābhyāṃ gṛhītvā yatnato 'pi ca 
agrato dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmaṃ vai pṛṣṭataḥ priye  SvaT 
muṣṭibhyāṃ saṃgṛhītvā vai uttānakarayogataḥ 
tato ghṛtena saṃplāvya abhimānaṃ tu kārayet  SvaT 
ahameva paraṃ tattvaṃ parāparavibhāgataḥ 
tattvamekaṃ hi sarvatra nānyaṃ bhāvaṃ tu kārayet  SvaT 
yatkumbhe 'dhvātra vinyastaḥ ṣaṭprakāro varānane 
maṇḍale 'gnau śiśorantaḥ sādhāraṇavikalpitaḥ  SvaT 
srucyadhvānaṃ tamāropya prāṇasthaṃ nāḍimadhyagam 
prāṇadhāre samīkṛtya srucā dhārāṃ vinikṣipet  SvaT 
vasudhāraprayogeṇa prakṣipejjātavedasi 
nābhisthāne sruco mūlaṃ nayannāsāntagocaram  SvaT 
yathā yathā tyajeddhārāṃ tathā prāṇaṃ samuccaret 
prāṇo 'pi varṇatāṃ yāti ṣaḍvidhādhvamayastu saḥ  SvaT 
ṣaḍvidhedhvani nāto 'nyaḥ prameyo vidyate kvacit 
tasmānmāntre parāmarśe heyopādeyataḥ sthitāḥ  SvaT 
varṇaiḥ kāraṇaṣaṭkaṃ tu ṣaṭtyāgātsaptame layaḥ 
akāraśca ukāraśca makāro bindureva ca  SvaT 
ardhacandro nirodhī ca nādaścaivordhvagāminī 
śaktiśca vyāpinī hyetāḥ samanā ca tataḥ param  SvaT 
samanāntaṃ varārohe pāśajālamanantakam 
kāraṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhirākrāntaṃ mantrasthaṃ heyalakṣaṇam  SvaT 
atra pāśopari hyātmā vyomavadbinduccitsunirmalaḥ 
śivatattvaguṇāmodāc chivadharmāvalokakaḥ  SvaT 
pāśāvalokanaṃ tyaktvā svarūpālokanaṃ hi yat 
ātmavyāptirbhavedeṣā śivavyāptistato 'nyathā  SvaT 
sarvajñyādiguṇā ye 'rthā vyāpakānbhāvayedyadā 
śivavyāptirbhavedeṣā caitanye heturūpiṇī  SvaT 
ato dharmisvabhāvo hi śivaḥ śāntaśca paṭhyate 
unmanāśca manogrāhyaḥ ātmabodhe sthitonmanāḥ  SvaT 
vyāpāraṃ mānasaṃ tyaktvā bodharūpeṇa yojayet 
tadā śivatvamāyāti paśurmukto bhavārṇavāt  SvaT 
pare caiva niyuktasya sruvamāpūrayetpunaḥ 
sruco randhreṇa taddravyaṃ yāvadvahnau prayujyate  SvaT 
bahisthāṃ kumbhakaṃ tāvat pare tattve tu bhāvayet 
bahirnirodhabhāvena sāmarasyaṃ śivena ca  SvaT 
anyathā na bhaveddevi nadīvega ivārṇave 
sthitaḥ sa sāgaredbhistu sindhuḥ samarasībhavet  SvaT 
punarvibhāgaṃ nāpnoti tathātmā tu śivārṇave 
srucastu pūraṇaṃ yāvat tāvatkālaṃ samādiśet  SvaT 
anenaiva tu kālena bahiḥ kumbhakavṛttinā 
ātmā samarasatvena śivībhavati sarvagaḥ  SvaT 
guṇānāpādayetpaścāt ṣaṭ aṅgaparimāhutīn 
yathā nṛpatve saṃprāpte kalaśaiścābhiṣicyate  SvaT 
vandibhiśca guṇāste 'pi khyāpyante vasudhātale 
tathā śivatve saṃprāpte guṇānāpādayedbudhaḥ  SvaT 
sarvajño vai bhava svāhā paritṛptastathaiva ca 
anādibodho bhava ca tataḥ svātantryaśaktikaḥ  SvaT 
tathā tvaluptaśaktiścā nantaśaktistataḥ punaḥ 
guṇānāpādya sarvāṃstān mūlamantramanusmaret  SvaT 
oṃhūmātmapadopetaṃ sarvajñāyetyapaścimam 
svāhākāraprayogeṇa āhutīḥ pratipādayet  SvaT 
tisraḥ pañca daśaikā vā tilairvātha ghṛtena vā 
dadyāt tato 'bhiṣekaṃ tu mūlamantreṇa suvrate  SvaT 
paraṃ śaktyamṛtaṃ kṣobhya śiṣyamūrdhni nipātayet 
turyadvāraṃ viśettaddhi sabāhyābhyantaraṃ smaret  SvaT 
mantraśaktibhirugrābhiḥ śeṣanirdahanādibhiḥ 
śarīraṃ śoṣyate tābhis tadarthamabhiṣecanam  SvaT 
dīkṣānirvartanātpūrvaṃ puṣpaṃ pāṇau pradāpayet 
darbhaṃ vimocayitvā ca śivāgnau kalaśe gurau  SvaT 
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā daṇḍavannipatedbhuvi 
kṛtakṛtyaḥ prahṛṣṭātmā bhavottīrṇaḥ sunirmalaḥ  SvaT 
protphullanayanaḥ śāntas tṛptātmānaṃ tu bhāvayet 
iyaṃ nairvāṇakī dīkṣā nirbījā vā sabījikā  SvaT 
yeṣāṃ sabījikā dīkṣā kuryātteṣvabhiṣecanam 
śrutaśīlasamācārān deśakatve niyojayet  SvaT 
athābhiṣeka ācārye śivayogādanantaram 
pañcabhiḥ kalaśairbhadre sitacandanalepitaiḥ  SvaT 
śivakumbhavadabhyarcya ratnagarbhāmbupūritaiḥ 
ṛddhivṛddhyādibhiḥ pūtair oṣadhyakṣatapūritaiḥ  SvaT 
sitapadmamukhodgāraiś cūtapallavasaṃyutaiḥ 
pṛthivyādīni tattvāni pañca pañcasu vinyaset  SvaT 
kalaśeṣu mahādevi punaścaiva kalā nyaset 
nivṛttyādyāḥ kalāḥ pañca teṣu caivātra vinyaset  SvaT 
ekaikakalaśo vyāpyo hy anantādiśivāntakaḥ 
pūjayedbhairavaṃ devaṃ sarvasaṃbhārakaiḥ kramāt  SvaT 
ṣaḍaṅgāvaraṇopetaṃ mantrasaṃdhānasaṃyutam 
bhairaveṇābhimantreta ekaikaṃ kalaśaṃ priye  SvaT 
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva paratattvamanusmaran 
vāruṇyāṃ saumyayamyāyam endryāmaiśyāṃ tathaiva ca  SvaT 
saṃpūjyaivaṃ vidhānena abhiṣekaṃ samācaret 
yāgaharmyasya aiśānyāṃ pīṭhaṃ saṃkalpyayebudhaḥ  SvaT 
tatra maṇḍalakaṃ kṛtvā svastikādivibhūṣitam 
vitānoparisaṃchannaṃ dhvajaiśca pariśobhitam  SvaT 
tatrāsanaṃ nyaseddevi śrīparṇīcandanodbhavam 
tatrānantāsanaṃ nyasya mūrtibhūtaṃ śiśuṃ nyaset  SvaT 
pūrvavatsakalīkṛtya aiśānyabhimukhaṃ sthitam 
gandhapuṣpādinābhyarcya nirbhartsyaḥ kāñcikaudanaiḥ  SvaT 
mṛdbhasmagomayaiḥ piṇḍair dūrvāṅkurasamāśritaiḥ 
siddhārthadadhitoyaiśca nirājanasamanvitaiḥ  SvaT 
nirbhartsyaivaṃ vidhānena abhiṣekaṃ pradāpayet 
pṛthivyādighaṭāsayirvā dhāmānusmṛtya secayet  SvaT 
kramāddhyātvā kalaśeṣu ācāryaḥ susamāhitaḥ 
abhiṣikto 'nyavāsastu paridhāpyācanettataḥ  SvaT 
praviśya dakṣiṇāṃ mūrtiṃ yogapīṭhaṃ prakalpayet
